<p><span class="font49">whenever </span><span class="font50">min (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t<sub>e</sub></span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">1</span><span class="font2"><sub>t</sub></span><span class="font3"><sub>-</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>) </span><span class="font51">≥ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font50">min (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font3"><sub>-</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>) </span><span class="font51">≥ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font46">&lt;</span><span class="font33">t</span><span class="font46">&lt;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font45"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1</span><span class="font46">&lt;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">&lt;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">q</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">for </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font51"> &gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font49">. Let us chose for </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font51">≤ £ ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49"> and</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font51">≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">1<sub>1</sub></span><span class="font50"> :</span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>e</sub></span><span class="font50"> / </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font50"> :</span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>k</sub>∕ n</span><span class="font49">, where </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>e</sub></span></p>
<p><span class="font45">'</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font49"> are integers that satisfy the conditions</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">0 </span><span class="font50">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>r</sub>.</span><span class="font50"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">m.</span><span class="font50"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font35" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font50"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font50"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font50"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font5">. </span><span class="font50">&lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font50"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">, 0 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">£ -</span><span class="font49">1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font5"><sup>t</sup> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">'' &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;' &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;' &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;'</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">0 </span><span class="font50">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50"> „ &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50">, &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font35" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font50"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">m„</span><span class="font50"> , &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">m„</span><span class="font50"> &lt;&nbsp;... &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> .</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">0 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font5">L </span><span class="font50">-</span><span class="font49">1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font5">L </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">q</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Then by the definition of partial sums, we get</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">p</span><span class="font21" style="font-style:italic;"> <sup>1</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">W (</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">.</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font46">×</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">.</span><span class="font50"> ),</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50">2) </span><span class="font51">≥ </span><span class="font50">3</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font31">}</span></p>

</div><br clear="all">

<p><span class="font14"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n <sup>S</sup></span><span class="font4">[</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">nt</span><span class="font45"> <sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font4">][</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ns</span><span class="font45"> <sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font4">]</span><span class="font45"><sup>,</sup> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n <sup>S</sup></span><span class="font4">[</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">nt</span><span class="font45"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font4">][</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ns</span><span class="font45"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font4">] </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n <sup>S</sup></span><span class="font4">[</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">nt</span><span class="font45"> <sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font4">][</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ns</span><span class="font45"> <sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font4">] </span><span class="font19"><sup>+</sup> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n <sup>S</sup></span><span class="font4">[</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">nt</span><span class="font45"> <sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font4">][</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ns</span><span class="font45"> <sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font4">] </span><span class="font49">Z </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">--DD</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">→</span></p>

<p><span class="font49">The result follows since</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">

<p><span class="font51">V <sup>[</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>o</sup>,</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font43">2 </span><span class="font45">W<sup>0</sup>,</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>s</sup></span><span class="font43"> 2 </span><span class="font48">]</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">whenever &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>e</sub></span><span class="font50"> / </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>t</sub></span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>-</sub></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>1</sub></span><span class="font50"> / </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font49"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>l</sub></span><span class="font50"> /</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>l</sub></span><span class="font3"><sub>-</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> /</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font49">, for </span><span class="font50">1 </span><span class="font51">&lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font51"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50">1 </span><span class="font51">&lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font49"> , </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">l</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">where </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>t</sub></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>k</sub></span><span class="font50"> :</span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">.</span><span class="font58"> ∑ ∑ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>j</sub></span><span class="font49"> . But by the independence </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font45">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">of {f</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font50"> :1 </span><span class="font51">≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font14">}</span><span class="font49">, we further get</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">p</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">W</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">.</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font50">, (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">×</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font50"> ),</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50">2) </span><span class="font51">≥ </span><span class="font50">3</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font31">}</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">q p</span><span class="font49"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;...</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">≤V V</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font51">^ </span><span class="font50">max </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">S<sub>11</sub> </span><span class="font51">≥</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font27" style="font-style:italic;">∖</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">⅛ I=</span><span class="font45">T &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>i</sup></span><span class="font43">1</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font51">t</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font51">t</span><span class="font1">-</span><span class="font43">1</span><span class="font45">) <sup>1</sup></span><span class="font43">2<sup>l</sup></span></p>

<p><span class="font51">Ν </span><span class="font50">0, &nbsp;</span><span class="font58">∫ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h d</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font50"> , </span><span class="font51">Ν </span><span class="font50">0, &nbsp;</span><span class="font58">∫ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h d</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">I</span></p>

<p><span class="font49">has the</span></p>

<div>
<p><span class="font51">V &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font45">0,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font43">1</span><span class="font48">]</span><span class="font43">×</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font45">0, </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font48">j &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font27" style="font-variant:small-caps;">j</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font51">V</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">same distribution</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font45">0,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">1</span><span class="font43">2 </span><span class="font48">]</span><span class="font43">×</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font45">0, </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font43"> 2 </span><span class="font48">] </span><span class="font7" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">J<sub>j</sub></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">with the</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font11">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B<sub>h</sub></span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font50">),</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B<sub>h</sub></span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">1</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub>,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s<sub>2</sub>))</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font49"> . The other cases handled analogously. Thus the assertion</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">vector can be for two</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">points follows. The set of three or more points can be treated in the same way, and hence the finite dimensional distributions of</span></p>
<p><span class="font20"><sup>{</sup></span><span class="font49"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Tn</span><span class="font49"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">En</span><span class="font50">×</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"><sup>)(</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font49"><sup>, </sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>s</sup></span><span class="font49"><sup>): (t,s)</sup> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font18">} </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n <sup>j</sup>n</span><span class="font50"> ≥</span><span class="font49">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">converges properly.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">To prove the second condition we apply the following auxiliary result. For any family of rectangles</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">For further simplification we chose </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>e</sub></span><span class="font50"> :</span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font50"> :</span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">km</span><span class="font50">' </span><span class="font49">for some integers </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50">' </span><span class="font49">that satisfy </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>t</sub></span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>t</sub></span><span class="font3"><sub>-</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font3"><sub>-</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50">'</span><span class="font51">≥ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ,</span><span class="font49"> for </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font51">≤ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font51"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font51">≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font49"> . Since the indexes </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font49"> must satisfy </span><span class="font50">( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50">1)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font51"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">pm</span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font50">1)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50">' </span><span class="font51">&lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">pm</span><span class="font50">'</span><span class="font49">, we chose</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font50"> :</span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font28">P</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> / </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font28"> ∖ —</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:line-through;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:line-through;">—</span><span class="font51" style="text-decoration:line-through;"> —</span><span class="font50"> 1/ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font51"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">2 / </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ </span><span class="font49">and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font50"> :</span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font28">P</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> / </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50">'</span><span class="font28">∖ —</span><span class="font51">——→ </span><span class="font50">1/ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font51"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">2 / </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font49">. Moreover, since</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">/</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font51"> ———→</span><span class="font50">1/</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font51"> &gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">1∕2</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span></p>

<div>

</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">

<div>
<p><span class="font49">0 </span><span class="font50">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49">0 </span><span class="font50">&lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font5">L </span><span class="font50">&lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>S</sub>q</span><span class="font50"> = </span><span class="font49">1, it holds:</span></p>

<div>

<div>
<p><span class="font50">max </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font31">{ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>λ </sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"><sup>mm</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>'</sup> </span><span class="font31">} &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">is</span></p>
<p><span class="font45">0</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font1" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font2" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>l</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font45"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3</span></p>
<p><span class="font45">0</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46"> ≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">'</span></p>

<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">. 10</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ <sub>D</sub>\</span><span class="font46"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;. r—</span><span class="font51">I</span></p>

<p><span class="font51">≤ </span><span class="font50">48</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>λ</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font50">max </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font15">{ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>λ </sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>mm</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>'</sup> </span><span class="font15">}</span></p>
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font45">2 0</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font1" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font2" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>l</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font45"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3</span></p>
<p><span class="font45">0</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">'</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">which directly implies that</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">lim lim sup </span><span class="font45"><sup>48</sup> </span><span class="font50">max </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font13">{ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>λ</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>n</sup> </span><span class="font13">}</span></p>
<p><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font46">→∞ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font3"><sub>→∞</sub> </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font45">2 0</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font1" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font2" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>l</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font45"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3</span></p>
<p><span class="font45">0</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">where </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50">:</span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font50">/ 2</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font49">. The last inequality follows from Etemadi’s inequality (Billingsley, 1995, Theorem 22.5). Thus the second condition will follow if we can show that</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">limlimsup &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;max </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font31">{ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>λ </sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>mm</sup></span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>'</sup></span><span class="font31">}</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">0</span><span class="font49">,</span></p>
<p><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font46">→∞ &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font45">2 0</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font1" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font2" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>l</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font45"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>,</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup> →</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45">0</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46"> ≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">'</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">which is the same with the condition</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">limlimsup max </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font13">{ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"><sup>λ</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font13"> } </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>λ</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>→∞</sup> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">'</span><span class="font46">→∞ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font45"><sup>2 0</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>≤</sup></span><span class="font2" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>l</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>≤</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</sup></span><span class="font2" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>l</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>,</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup> →</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45">0</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46"> ≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">'</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">By the Lindeberg’s central limit theorem and Chebyshev’s inequality, if </span><span class="font35" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font4" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>λ</sub></span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>λ</sub></span><span class="font49"> are large enough such that </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>λ</sub></span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>λ</sub></span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> , then we have</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">[ </span><span class="font58">∫</span><span class="font50">9</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">hd</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">≤ &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">lim limsup max </span><span class="font37"><sup>[</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>0,</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>]×[</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>0,</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>s</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>]</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">λ→∞ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font46">→∞ &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50"> n</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font50">9</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font49">This complete the proof of the theorem. ■</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Corollary 1. </span><span class="font49">Let (</span><span class="font50">Ξ</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">) be a metric space with metric </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49"> , and let </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font49"> be the Borel </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font49"> -algebra over</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font49"> . If </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font49"> : </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">C</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font50">→ Ξ </span><span class="font49">is continuous on </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">C</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49">) , then</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">g fa </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">e</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"> En</span><span class="font50"> × </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">)) </span><span class="font51">——→ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">g </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">b</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"> Bh</span><span class="font49">),</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">as </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> → ∞ </span><span class="font49">.</span></p>

<p><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>λ</sub></span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>λ</sub></span><span class="font49">, where </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>λ</sub></span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>λ</sub></span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> , Chebyshev’s inequality gives the inequality</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark21"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark22"></a>4. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SIMULATION</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Based on Theorem 3.1 we can approximate the sample paths of </span><span class="font11">{</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B<sub>h</sub></span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">) : (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font11">} </span><span class="font49">with those of</span></p>
<div>
<h3><a name="bookmark23"></a><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;"><a name="bookmark24"></a>p</span><span class="font13" style="font-style:italic;"> {</span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">∖</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font33">,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font27">∣</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">■</span><span class="font13"> }</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">p.</span></h3>

<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font1" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span></p>
<p><span class="font58">∑ </span><span class="font58" style="font-style:italic;">∑</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>j</sub></span></p>

<p><span class="font50">9</span><span class="font58">∑ ∑ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> /</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font50"> /</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50">)</span></p>

<h2><a name="bookmark25"></a><span class="font19"><sup><a name="bookmark26"></a>≤</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45">42</span></h2>
<h3><a name="bookmark27"></a><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><a name="bookmark28"></a>n</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span></h3>
<p><span class="font7"><sub>≤</sub> </span><span class="font50">9</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45"><sup>2 ,</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">where </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49"> is the bound of the function </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font49"> .</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Consequently,</span></p>
<div><img src="https://jurnal.harianregional.com/media/2908-4.png" alt="" style="width:101pt;height:92pt;">
<p><span class="font2">N=30, e_ij~N(0,ij/n^2)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div><img src="https://jurnal.harianregional.com/media/2908-5.png" alt="" style="width:100pt;height:86pt;">
<p><span class="font2">N=40, e_ij~N(0,ij/n^2)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">variance given by the function </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ts</span><span class="font49"> , for </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font36" style="font-weight:bold;">Begin algorithm</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div><img src="https://jurnal.harianregional.com/media/2908-6.png" alt="" style="width:210pt;height:78pt;">
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Figure 1. Approximated sample paths of</span></p>
<p><span class="font11">{</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">):(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font11">}</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">The simulation is developed by using the software package S-PLUS for several sample sizes, i.e., </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> = 20, 25, 30 and 40 in which the components of </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">En</span><span class="font50">×</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>n</sub></span><span class="font49"> are generated from normal distribution with mean zero and variance given by the function </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ts</span><span class="font49"> , for </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49">. The figure shows that the sample paths of </span><span class="font11">{</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B<sub>h</sub></span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">):(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font11">} </span><span class="font49">are typically unbounded in variation as well as not differentiable on I.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">By Corollary 1, we can also approximate the quantiles of the statistics </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font49"> , </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">KS</span><span class="font49"> , and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">CR</span><span class="font49"> defined in Section 1 by using Monte Carlo simulation by the fact that for n </span><span class="font50">→ ∞</span><span class="font49">,</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Step 1: Fixed </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">in </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">N</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Step 2: Generate </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49"> i.i.d. pseudo random matrices</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">En</span><span class="font50">×</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> whose components in the </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">t h row and </span><span class="font35" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font49"> th column are generated from</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">N</span><span class="font15" style="font-variant:small-caps;">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-variant:small-caps;">o, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">h </span><span class="font15" style="font-variant:small-caps;">(</span><span class="font5" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>l</sup></span><span class="font49"> ,</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font18">))</span><span class="font49">, 1 </span><span class="font50">≤ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font50"> ≤ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49"> . </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">nn</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Step 3: Calculate</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Kn</span><span class="font49">^<sup>:</sup></span><span class="font50">=,</span><span class="font49">^max <sup>-</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Tn</span><span class="font49"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">En</span><span class="font50">×</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"><sup>)(</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">’</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">)' 1</span><span class="font50">≤</span><span class="font5">L</span><span class="font49">,</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50">≤</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n n</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Step 4: Calculate the simulated (1 </span><span class="font50">— </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font49">) -quantiles of</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font49">: Sort all </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49"> values of </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">K<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font49"><sup>( </sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>j</sup></span><span class="font49"><sup>)</sup> in ascending order. Let </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">K<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font49"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>M</sup></span><span class="font49"><sup>: </sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>j</sup></span><span class="font49"><sup>)</sup> be the </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49">’th smallest value, (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49">:1) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49">:</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49"> )</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">i.e. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Kn </span><span class="font50">' ≤ </span><span class="font5">L </span><span class="font50">≤ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">κn s</span><span class="font49"> , the simulated (1 </span><span class="font50">— </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font49">) of K is given by</span></p>

<div>
<h4><a name="bookmark29"></a><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup><a name="bookmark30"></a>c</sup></span><span class="font49">1</span><span class="font50">—</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font51"> <sup>:</sup>= 1</span></h4>

<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49">∙</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49">(1</span><span class="font50">—</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font49">))</span></p>

<p><span class="font13">„ (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49"> : </span><span class="font11">[</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49">(1 </span><span class="font50">— </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font11">]</span><span class="font13">)</span><span class="font50">+</span><span class="font49">1 &nbsp;&nbsp;<sub>1</sub></span></p>

<p><span class="font51">(</span><span class="font49">1 </span><span class="font50">≤</span><span class="font5">L</span><span class="font49">,</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">≤</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">nn <sup>n n</sup></span><span class="font50">×</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n nn</sup></span></p>

<p><span class="font49">1</span><span class="font50">≤</span><span class="font5">L</span><span class="font49">,</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50">≤</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">nn <sup>n n</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">×</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n nn</sup></span></p><img src="https://jurnal.harianregional.com/media/2908-7.png" alt="" style="width:19pt;height:34pt;">

<p><span class="font61">-1 </span><span class="font50">∑ ∑ </span><span class="font61">(</span><span class="font49"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font49"> )(</span><span class="font5"><sup>L</sup></span><span class="font49">,</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font61">)</span><span class="font49"><sup>2</sup> &gt;</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">^</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>n</sub></span><span class="font49"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50">=</span><span class="font49">0</span><span class="font5">L</span><span class="font50">=</span><span class="font49">0</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">nn <sup>n n</sup> n n'n</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">≥</span></p>

<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">-D</span><span class="font51">→ </span><span class="font49">sup </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49">,</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49">), 0</span><span class="font50">≤ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">≤</span><span class="font49">1 </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">h</span></p>

<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">-D</span><span class="font51">→∫</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">b</span><span class="font49" style="font-variant:small-caps;">2 </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">(t</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s)λj</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">dt, ds)</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>

<div>
<p><span class="font49">The following algorithm is applied to approximate </span><span class="font50">(1 </span><span class="font51">— </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">×</span><span class="font50">100% </span><span class="font49">quantiles of the Kolmogorov type statistic (K), for preassigned values of </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50">(0,1) </span><span class="font49">. The simulation results developed by using the software package S-PLUS for the statistics K , KS and CR under several choices of sample sizes and </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font49">are presented in Table 1. For the simulation we generate the components of </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font6"><sub>×</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>n </sub></span><span class="font49">from normal distribution with mean zero and</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font36" style="font-weight:bold;">End algorithm</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">We note that the algorithm is given for the Kolmogorov type statistic only since the algorithm for other statistics can be constructed analogously. The constants </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font49"><sup>~</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font49"><sup>~</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;, and <sup>~</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;presented in</span></p>
<h4><a name="bookmark31"></a><span class="font51"><a name="bookmark32"></a>t</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font51"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;t</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font51"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;t</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">α</span></h4>
<p><span class="font49">Table 1 are real numbers that satisfy the conditions</span></p>

<h6><a name="bookmark37"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark38"></a>5. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CONCLUSION</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">The stochastic process </span><span class="font11">{</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font50">):(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t,s</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font11">} </span><span class="font49">can be constructed as the limit process of the sequence</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">1</span><span class="font49"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font49"><sub>1</sub> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">En×„«t</span><span class="font49"> ∙ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49"><sup>):</sup> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49"> ■ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font51"> }</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">[ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n n n </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">× </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">nn</span><span class="font50">≥</span><span class="font49">ι</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">by applying the Lindeberg’s central limit theorem and the notion of weak convergence of a sequence of probability measures on a metric space. It is also shown by this result that the </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font49"> -generalized standard Brownian sheet exists. As by products the quantiles of the Kolmogorov, Kolmogorov-Smirnov and Cramér-von Mises type statistics which are very important in change-point as well as in model-check problems can be approximated by simulation.</span></p>

<h6><a name="bookmark41"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark42"></a>INTISARI</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">Makalah ini membahas tentang pemodelan dan penentuan waktu penyelesaian siklus (</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">cycle</span><span class="font48">) layanan jaringan antrian fork-join taksiklik dengan kapasitas penyangga takhingga, dengan menggunakan aljabar </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font48">. Hasil pembahasan menunjukkan bahwa dinamika jaringan antrian fork-join taksiklik dengan kapasitas penyangga takhingga dapat dimodelkan ke dalam suatu persamaan matriks atas aljabar </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font48">. Dapat ditunjukkan pula bahwa waktu siklus layanan jaringan antrian merupakan eigennilai </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font48"> dari matriks pada persamaan tersebut.dsfsdlkslkflskfslkflkflsdkfjlskflskjflsdlkjlklkl</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Kata kunci: aljabar max-plus, eigennilai max-plus, jaringan antrian fork-join, waktu penyelesaian siklus layanan.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark43"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark44"></a>MAX-PLUS ALGEBRA MODELLING AND PERFORMANCE EVALUATION OF QUEUEING NONCYCLIC FORK-JOIN NETWORK WITH INFITE BUFFER CAPACITY</span></h6>
<p><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font49">M. ANDY RUDHITO, </span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font49">SRI WAHYUNI, </span><span class="font45"><sup>3</sup></span><span class="font49">ARI SUPARWANTO, DAN </span><span class="font45"><sup>4</sup></span><span class="font49">F. SUSILO</span></p>
<p><span class="font48"><sup>1</sup>PhD Students at Mathematics Department,FMIPA, UGM and Lecturer at FKIP, Sanata Dharma University, Yogyakarta</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font48"><sup>2,3</sup> Mathematics Department, FMIPA, Gadjah Mada University, Yogyakarta</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font48"><sup>4</sup>Mathematics Department, FST, Sanata Dharma University,Yogyakarta</span></p>
<p><span class="font47">Email : </span><a href="mailto:1rudhito@staff.usd.ac.id"><span class="font47"><sup>1</sup>rudhito@staff.usd.ac.id</span></a><span class="font47">, </span><a href="mailto:2swahyuni@ugm.ac.id"><span class="font47"><sup>2</sup>swahyuni@ugm.ac.id</span></a><span class="font47">, </span><a href="mailto:3ari_suparwanto@yahoo.com"><span class="font47"><sup>3</sup>ari_suparwanto@yahoo.com</span></a><span class="font47">, </span><a href="mailto:4fsusilo@staff.usd.ac.id"><span class="font47"><sup>4</sup>fsusilo@staff.usd.ac.id</span></a></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark45"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark46"></a>ABSTRACT</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">This paper aims to model and determine the service cycle completion time of noncyclic fork-join queueing networks with infinite buffer capacity, using max-plus algebra. The finding show that the dynamics of the noncyclic fork-join queuing networks with infinite buffer capacity can be modeled into a matrix equation over max-plus algebra. We can also show that the service cycle completion time of queuing networks is a max-plus eigenvalues of the matrix in the equation.slklsklslsllsllllllllllllllllllllll</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Keywords: max-plus algebra, max-plus eigenvalues, fork-join queueing networks, service cycle completion time.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark47"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark48"></a>1. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PENDAHULUAN</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Jaringan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">fork-join</span><span class="font49"> merupakan salah satu sistem antrian yang memungkinkan pelanggan (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">customer</span><span class="font49">) terpecah menjadi beberapa bagian, dan digabung kembali menjadi satu setelah pelanggan melalui sistem tersebut. Sistem seperti ini banyak dijumpai pada proses produksi dalam industri, pengiriman pesan dalam jaringan komunikasi, dan pemrosesan data dalam sistem komputer multiprosesor. Sebagai gambaran dalam jaringan komunikasi, pesan terpecah menjadi paket-paket yang disampaikan melalui jalur</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">terpisah, kemudian digabungkan kembali di titik tujuan jaringan tersebut hingga diperoleh pesan seperti semula.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Dalam pembahasan jaringan antrian dapat diasumsikan bahwa kapasitas penyangga (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">buffer</span><span class="font49">) takhingga atau berhingga. Pemodelan dinamika jaringan dengan menggunakan aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus </span><span class="font49">dapat memberikan deskripsi yang lebih kompak dan terpadu (Baccelli </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49">, 1992). Di samping itu pemodelan ini juga memudahkan dalam hal komputasi numeriknya. Pemodelan jaringan antrian dengan menggunakan aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font49"> telah mulai</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dibahas dalam Krivulin (1994, 1995, 1996a, 1996b). Dalam Krivulin (1994) telah dibahas pemodelan untuk antrian jenis G/G/1. Pemodelan dan evaluasi kinerja, yang meliputi waktu sistem pelanggan dan waktu tunggu pelanggan, untuk sistem antrian </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">tandem</span><span class="font49"> telah dibahas dalam Krivulin (1995). Dalam literatur tersebut pembahasan secara eksplisit baru dibahas untuk sistem antrian </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">tandem</span><span class="font49"> dengan kapasitas penyangga takhingga. Dalam Krivulin (1996a) untuk jaringan antrian </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">fork-join</span><span class="font49"> taksiklik dengan kapasitas penyangga takhingga telah diberikan persamaan dinamika keadaan (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">state dynamic equation</span><span class="font49">) secara eksplisit, dan sistem antrian </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">tandem</span><span class="font49"> dipandang sebagai kejadian khususnya</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">.</span><span class="font49"> Persamaan keadaan dinamik secara eksplisit untuk jaringan antrian </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">fork-join</span><span class="font49"> taksiklik dengan kapasitas penyangga berhingga telah diberikan dalam Krivulin (1996b). Pemodelan yang dilakukan dalam Krivulin (1996a, 1996b), diasumsikan bahwa pada waktu awal jaringan beroperasi, penyangga tidak selalu kosong.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Makalah ini akan membahas pemodelan dan kinerja (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">performance</span><span class="font49">) jaringan antrian </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">fork-join </span><span class="font49">taksiklik dengan kapasitas penyangga takhingga, dengan kondisi pada awal jaringan beroperasi, penyangga dalam keadaan kosong. Pemodelan dilakukan dengan pendekatan aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font49">. Kinerja jaringan yang dibahas adalah analisis waktu penyelesaian siklus layanan jaringan antrian dikaitkan dengan eigennilaialjabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark49"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark50"></a>2. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ALJABAR </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">MAX-PLUS</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> DAN TEORI GRAF</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Dalam bagian ini dibahas konsep dasar aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font49"> dan kaitannya dengan teori graf yang akan digunakan dalam pembahasan untuk bagian-bagian selanjutnya. Materi lebih lengkap dapat dilihat pada Baccelli </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (1992), Krivulin (1996b), dan Rudhito (2003).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Diberikan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> : = </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R </span><span class="font26">∪</span><span class="font49">{</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> } dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R </span><span class="font49">adalah himpunan semua bilangan real dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> : = </span><span class="font50">-∞</span><span class="font49">. Pada </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>ε</sub></span><span class="font49"> didefinisikan operasi berikut: </span><span class="font26">∀</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a,b</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>ε</sub></span><span class="font49"> , </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">b </span><span class="font49">:= max(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a, b</span><span class="font49">) dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49"> : = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49"> + </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49">. (</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font49">) merupakan semigelanggang komutatif idempoten dengan elemen netral </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font50">-∞ </span><span class="font49">dan elemen satuan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font49"> = 0, yaitu bahwa </span><span class="font26">∀</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a,b</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>ε</sub></span><span class="font49"> berlaku:</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49">i)</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49">, (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font49">), </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49">.</span></p></li>
<li>
<p><span class="font49">ii) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font49">) , </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49"> + 0 = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49"> = 0 + </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49">.</span></p></li>

<p><span class="font49">Lebih lanjut (</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>ε</sub></span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font49">) merupakan semilapangan (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">semifield</span><span class="font49">), yaitu bahwa (</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font49">) merupakan semigelanggang (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">semigelanggang</span><span class="font49">) komutatif dengan kondisi untuk setiap </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R </span><span class="font49">terdapat </span><span class="font50">-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49"> sehingga berlaku </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font50">-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49">) = 0. </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font45">max </span><span class="font49">: = (</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font49">) disebut dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">aljabar max-plus</span><span class="font49">, yang selanjutnya cukup dituliskan dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">. Dalam hal urutan pengoperasian (jika tanda kurang tidak dituliskan), operasi </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">mempunyai prioritas yang lebih tinggi dari pada operasi </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49">. Pangkat </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> dari elemen </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R </span><span class="font49">dinotasikan dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">didefinisikan sebagai berikut:</span></p>
<p><span class="font46">0</span></p>

<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49"> : = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49"> ,</span></p>

<p><span class="font49">Operasi </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">pada </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font45">max </span><span class="font49">di atas dapat</span></p>

Khususnya untuk matriks dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n </sup></span><span class="font45">max &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;max</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">didefinisikan</span></p>

<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>

<p><span class="font9" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font45">ma</span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font45">x</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font49"> , (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> )</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ij</span><span class="font49"> := </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">untuk setiap </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49"> . (</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font49">) merupakan semigelanggang &nbsp;(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">semiring</span><span class="font49">) idempoten dengan</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">elemen netral matriks </span><span class="font9" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> dan elemen satuan matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font49">.
