Pangkat </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> dari matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>x</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">dalam aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font49"> didefinisikan dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>0</sup> </span><span class="font49">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font49">untuk </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> = 1, 2, .... Selanjutnya akibat sifat idempoten operasi </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49">, untuk setiap </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>nxn</sup></span><span class="font49"> berlaku (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>q</sup></span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">... </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A<sup>q</sup></span><span class="font49">. </span><span class="font45">max</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Suatu </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">graf berarah G</span><span class="font49"> didefinisikan sebagai suatu pasangan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> = (</span><span class="font36">V, A</span><span class="font49">) dengan </span><span class="font36">V </span><span class="font49">adalah suatu himpunan berhingga takkosong yang anggotanya disebut </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">titik</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font36">A </span><span class="font49">adalah suatu himpunan pasangan terurut titik-titik. Anggota </span><span class="font36">A </span><span class="font49">disebut </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">busur</span><span class="font49">. Suatu </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">lintasan</span><span class="font49"> dalam graf berarah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> adalah suatu barisan berhingga busur (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font49">), (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45">3</span><span class="font49">), ... , (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font49">) dengan (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">,</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>k+</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub></span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font36">A </span><span class="font49">untuk suatu </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> Ν </span><span class="font49">(= himpunan semua bilangan asli), dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> = 1, 2, ... , </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font50"> - </span><span class="font49">1. Untuk suatu lintasan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">panjang lintasan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font49"> didefinisikan sebagai banyak busur yang menyusun </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font49"> dan dinotasikan dengan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>l</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> . </span><span class="font49">Suatu lintasan disebut </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">sirkuit</span><span class="font49"> jika titik awal dan titik akhirnya sama. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Sirkuit elementer </span><span class="font49">adalah sirkuit yang titik-titiknya muncul tidak lebih dari sekali, kecuali titik awal yang muncul tepat dua kali. Suatu graf berarah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> = (</span><span class="font36">V, A</span><span class="font49">) dengan </span><span class="font36">V </span><span class="font49">= {</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">1</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">2</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font49"> , ... , </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">n</span><span class="font49">} dikatakan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">terhubung kuat</span><span class="font49"> jika untuk setiap </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">i</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> j </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font36">V </span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">i </span><span class="font50">≠ </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">j </span><span class="font49">, terdapat suatu lintasan dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">i </span><span class="font49">ke </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">j </span><span class="font49">. Suatu graf yang memuat sirkuit disebut </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">graf siklik</span><span class="font49">, sedangkan suatu graf yang tidak memuat sirkuit disebut </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">graf taksiklik</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Untuk setiap graf berarah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> = (</span><span class="font36">V, A</span><span class="font49">) dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font49">titik, didefinisikan suatu matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">, yang disebut dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">matriks kedampingan</span><span class="font49"> dari graf berarah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> , dengan unsur-unsurnya adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">0, jika ( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50">A;</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font50">, jika (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∉</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50">A.</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font51">i</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font49">Diberikan graf berarah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> = (</span><span class="font36">V, A</span><span class="font49">) dengan </span><span class="font36">V </span><span class="font49">= {</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">1</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> 2</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">, ...</span><span class="font49"> , </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">p</span><span class="font49">}. Graf berarah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> dikatakan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">berbobot</span><span class="font49"> jika setiap busur (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font36">A </span><span class="font49">dikawankan dengan suatu bilangan real </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49">. Bilangan real </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49"> disebut </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">bobot </span><span class="font49">busur (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">), dinotasikan dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">). Dalam penyajiannya dengan gambar untuk graf berarah berbobot, busur diberi label dengan bobotnya. Didefinisikan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">graf preseden</span><span class="font49"> dari matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x </sub></span><span class="font49">adalah graf berarah berbobot </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) = (</span><span class="font36">V, A</span><span class="font49">) dengan </span><span class="font36">V </span><span class="font49">= {</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">1</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">2</span><span class="font49">, ... , </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">n</span><span class="font49">}, </span><span class="font36">A </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">=</span><span class="font49"> {(</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">j</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">i</span><span class="font49">) | </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">i</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">j</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">ij </span><span class="font50">≠ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> }. Perhatikan sebaliknya bahwa untuk setiap graf berarah berbobot </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> = (</span><span class="font36">V, A</span><span class="font49">) selalu dapat didefinisikan suatu matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">, dengan</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">W j</span><span class="font8">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font8">), </span><span class="font50">jika (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font8">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font8">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font8">A </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font50"> jika (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font8">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∉</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font8">A</span><span class="font50">.</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font51">‘</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font49">Jelas bahwa graf berarah berbobot tersebut merupakan graf preseden dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Diberikan graf berarah berbobot </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> = (</span><span class="font36">V, A</span><span class="font49">) dengan </span><span class="font36">V </span><span class="font49">= {</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">1</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">2</span><span class="font49">, ... , </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">n</span><span class="font49">}. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Bobot suatu lintasan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font50">→ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> → </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">... </span><span class="font50">→ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>l</sub></span><span class="font49"> didefinisikan sebagai jumlahan bobot busur-busur yang menyusun </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ρ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">.</span><span class="font49"> Bobot lintasan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font49"> dinotasikan dengan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>w</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> . </span><span class="font49">Untuk matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font49"> , bobot suatu lintasan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">lintasan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> → </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> → </span><span class="font45">max</span></p>
<p><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font50">→ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>l</sub></span><span class="font49"> dalam graf preseden </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) adalah </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>w</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> =</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> +</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> + </span><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font49">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> . Bobot rata-rata lintasan </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45"> 2 </span><span class="font4"><sup>,</sup> </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45">1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45"> 3 </span><span class="font4"><sup>,</sup> </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45"> 2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font4"><sup>,</sup> </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font45">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font49">, dinotasikan dengan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font49"> , didefinisikan sebagai</span></p><img src="https://jurnal.harianregional.com/media/2908-8.png" alt="" style="width:43pt;height:27pt;">
<p><span class="font49">Berikut diberikan suatu interpretasi dalam teori graf untuk pangkat </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">dalam aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font49">. Diberikan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">. Jika </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> Ν </span><span class="font49">,</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">maka unsur ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">st</span><span class="font49"> dari matriks </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49"> adalah </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font50"> )</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>st</sub></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">= </span><span class="font50">max </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> + </span><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font49">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> +</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> ) = </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font4"> ’ </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font45">1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font4"><sup>1</sup>2 ’ </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font4">’ </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">t'</span></p>
<p><span class="font46"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font24">≤</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font4"><sup>, </sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font45">2 </span><span class="font35" style="font-style:italic;">L</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font24">≤ </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">max </span><span class="font49">( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> +</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> +</span></p>
<p><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>1</sub> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;, &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;i</span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font4">, </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">t &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;i</span><span class="font45"> 2</span><span class="font4">, </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font46"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font24">≤</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font4"><sup>,</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font45">2 </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">Lik</span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font24">≤</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font49">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> ) untuk</span></p>
<p><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font4">, </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font45">-1 <sup>7</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font49">setiap </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49"><sup>,</sup> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49">. Karena ( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A<sub>1</sub></span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49"> + </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font4">, </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub></span><span class="font49">+ </span><span class="font0" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>l</sup></span><span class="font49"> + </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>A</sup></span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">si</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>k</sub></span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub></span><span class="font49">) adalah bobot lintasan dengan panjang </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t </span><span class="font49">sebagai titik awal dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49"> sebagai titik akhirnya dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">), maka </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font50"> )</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>st</sub></span><span class="font49"> adalah bobot maksimum semua lintasan dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) dengan panjang </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k,</span><span class="font49"> dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t </span><span class="font49">sebagai titik awal dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49"> sebagai titik akhirnya. Jika tidak ada lintasan dengan panjang </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49"> ke </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49">, maka bobot maksimum didefinisikan sama dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Sekarang diperhatikan bobot rata-rata maksimum sirkuit elementer, dengan maksimum diambil atas semua sirkuit elementer dalam graf. Diberikan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">dengan graf presedennya </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) = (</span><span class="font36">V, E </span><span class="font49">). Bobot maksimum dari semua sirkuit dengan panjang </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> dengan titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> sebagai titik awal dan titik akhir dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) dituliskan sebagai </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font50"> )</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>ii</sub></span><span class="font49"> . Maksimum dari bobot maksimum semua sirkuit dengan panjang </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> dengan titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> sebagai titik awal dan titik akhir </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>k </sub></span><span class="font49">dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) atas seluruh titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> adalah </span><span class="font42">⊕</span><span class="font58"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font37"> </span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>ii </sub></span><span class="font45">i</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font45">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">yang dapat dituliskan sebagai trace</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font50"> ) </span><span class="font49">dan rata-ratanya adalah </span><span class="font50">(1/</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50">) &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">trace(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49">) . Kemudian</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">diambil maksimum atas sirkuit dengan panjang </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> ≤ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">, yaitu atas semua sirkuit elementer, diperoleh suatu rumus untuk bobot rata-rata maksimum sirkuit elementer dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) (dinotasikan dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50"><sub>max</sub></span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">)), </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">sebagai berikut: </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50"><sub>max</sub></span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font42">⊕</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>k</sub></span><span class="font3"><sub>=</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">[(1/</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) trace</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font50"> ) </span><span class="font49">]</span><span class="font50"><sub>.</sub></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Suatu sirkuit dalam graf </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> disebut s</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">irkuit kritis </span><span class="font49">jika bobot rata-ratanya sama dengan bobot rata-rata maksimum sirkuit elementer dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G.</span><span class="font49"> Suatu graf yang terdiri dari semua sirkuit kritis dari graf </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G </span><span class="font49">disebut </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">graf kritis dari G</span><span class="font49"> dan dinotasikan dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G<sup>c</sup></span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Berikut diberikan definisi dan teorema yang pembuktiannya dapat dilihat dalam Rudhito (2003).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Teorema 1. (Baccelli, </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">et al.,</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> 2001). </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Diberikan A </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Jika semua sirkuit dalam G(A) mempunyai bobot nonpositif, maka</span></p>
<p><span class="font26">∀</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font50"> ≥ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> , </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>p</sup> </span><span class="font6" style="font-variant:small-caps;text-decoration:underline;">p</span><span class="font46">m </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">L</span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font46"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Bukti </span><span class="font49">: lihat Baccelli </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (2001) atau Rudhito (2003). &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;■</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Berdasarkan Teorema 1 di atas didefinisikan operasi bintang (</span><span class="font26">∗</span><span class="font49">) untuk matriks berikut ini.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Definisi 1. (Baccelli, </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">et.al.,</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> 2001) </span><span class="font49">Diberikan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">dengan semua sirkuit dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) mempunyai bobot nonpositif . Didefinisikan </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">n &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;n</span><span class="font24">+</span><span class="font46">1</span></p>
<h5><a name="bookmark51"></a><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><a name="bookmark52"></a>A</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> </span><span class="font49">: = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font49">dan</span></h5>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font45"><sup>+</sup> </span><span class="font49">: = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Definisi 2. </span><span class="font49">(Eigennilai dan eigenvektor aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">maxplus</span><span class="font49">). Diberikan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">. Skalar </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>max</sub></span><span class="font49"> disebut </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">eigennilai aljabar max-plus matriks A</span><span class="font49"> jika terdapat suatu vektor </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>max</sub> </span><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50"> ≠ </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>n</sub></span><span class="font3"><sub>×</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">sehingga </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">v.</span><span class="font49"> Vektor </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font49"> tersebut disebut </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">eigenvektor aljabar max-plus matriks A yang bersesuaian dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Berikut teorema yang memberikan eksistensi eigennilai aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font49"> untuk setiap </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Teorema 2. </span><span class="font49">(Baccelli, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.,</span><span class="font49"> 2001). </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Diberikan A </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">. Skalar </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">max</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">(A), yaitu bobot rata-rata maksimum sirkuit elementer dalam G(A), merupakan suatu eigennilai aljabar max-plus matriks A.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark53"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark54"></a>Bukti:</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">lihat Baccelli, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.,</span><span class="font49"> (2001) atau Rudhito (2003).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">■</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Dalam Rudhito (2003) dijelaskan bahwa jika titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> menyusun busur dalam sirkuit kritis </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ρ</span><span class="font45">0 </span><span class="font49">dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font4">*</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">, maka kolom ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> matriks </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font49"> merupakan eigenvektor yang bersesuaian dengan eigennilai </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">), dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font50">-</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">, dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> </span><span class="font49">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">B </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font24"> -</span><span class="font46">1</span></p>
<h5><a name="bookmark55"></a><span class="font26"><a name="bookmark56"></a>⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">.</span></h5>
<p><span class="font49">Berikut diberikan suatu teorema yang memberikan syarat perlu eigennilaialjabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus </span><span class="font49">suatu matriks.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Teorema 3. </span><span class="font49">( Baccelli, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et.al.,</span><span class="font49"> 2001) </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Diberikan A </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">. Jika skalar </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R, merupakan eigennilai aljabar max-plus matriks A, maka </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">merupakan bobot rata-rata suatu sirkuit dalam G(A).</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark57"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark58"></a>Bukti:</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">lihat Baccelli, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (2001) atau Rudhito (2003).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">■</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Dari Teorema 2 dan 3 dapat disimpulkan bahwa untuk </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>a</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"><sub>x</sub> </span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50"><sub>max</sub></span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) merupakan eigennilai aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font49"> maksimum matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">. Berikut diberikan lema-lema yang akan melandasi pembahasan selanjutnya.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Lema 4. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Jika A </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> R </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup> adalah matriks </span><span class="font45">max</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">kedampingan graf berarah taksiklik G, maka A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>q</sup> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">= </span><span class="font9" style="font-style:italic;">ε </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">, untuk semua q </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">&gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p, dengan p adalah panjang lintasan terpanjang dari G.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark59"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark60"></a>Bukti:</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Perhatikan bahwa untuk matriks kedampingan di atas, unsur ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">st</span><span class="font49"> dari matriks </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49"> adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font50">max </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> +</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font49">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> ), </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>st</sub> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45"><sub>1</sub> , </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">t &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;i</span><span class="font45"><sub>2</sub> , </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45"><sub>1</sub> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font45">, </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font1"><sub> -</sub></span><span class="font45"><sub>1</sub></span></p>
<p><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45"><sub>1</sub> ,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45"><sub>2</sub> ,</span><span class="font33">L</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font1"><sub>-</sub></span><span class="font45"><sub>1</sub></span><span class="font46">≤</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">untuk setiap </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49">. Perhatikan bahwa </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font50"> )</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>st</sub></span><span class="font50"> ≠ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> jika dan hanya jika ada sedikitnya satu lintasan dengan panjang </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">, dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49"> sebagai titik awal dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49"> sebagai titik akhirnya. Andaikan graf berarah di atas siklik, maka selalu dapat dibuat lintasan pada suatu sirkuitnya dengan panjang berapa pun. Hal ini berakibat bahwa </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>q</sup></span><span class="font50"> ≠ </span><span class="font9" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> , untuk semua </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font49"> = 1, 2, .... Jadi jika graf berarah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> di atas taksiklik, maka </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>q</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> = </span><span class="font9" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> , untuk semua </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font50"> &gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49">, dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49"> adalah panjang lintasan terpanjangnya. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;■</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Lema 5. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Diberikan A </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>×</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup> dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">R</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup> dengan </span><span class="font45">max &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;max</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">unsur-unsurnya positif atau sama dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">. Jika graf, dengan matriks A merupakan matriks kedampingannya, taksiklik, maka persamaan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">= A </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">⊗</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">⊕</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">mempunyai penyelesaian tunggal. Lebih lanjut penyelesaian diberikan oleh </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">= (E </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">⊕</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A)<sup>p</sup> </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">⊗</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">, dengan p adalah panjang lintasan terpanjang dalam graf tersebut.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark61"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark62"></a>Bukti:</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Dengan mensubstitusikan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49"> pada persamaan di atas sebanyak </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font49"> kali (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font50"> &gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49">) diperoleh</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Substitusi ke-1 :</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b</span></p>
<p><span class="font47">2</span></p>
<h5><a name="bookmark63"></a><span class="font49"><a name="bookmark64"></a>= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b</span></h5>
<p><span class="font47">2</span></p>
<h5><a name="bookmark65"></a><span class="font49"><a name="bookmark66"></a>= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">.</span></h5>
<p><span class="font49">Substitusi ke-2 :</span></p>
<h5><a name="bookmark67"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;"><a name="bookmark68"></a>x</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49"><sup>3</sup></span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font26"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49"><sup>2</sup>) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">.</span></h5>
<p><span class="font49">Substitusi ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font49"> :</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font23"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>q</sup></span><span class="font23"><sup>+</sup></span><span class="font46"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font23"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>q</sup></span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49">. Mengingat graf di atas taksiklik maka </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>q</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> = </span><span class="font9" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> , untuk semua </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font50"> &gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49">, sehingga diperoleh</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49"> = (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font52">L</span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font23"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>p</sup></span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49"> = (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>p</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Dari proses mencari penentuan penyelesaian di atas nampak bahwa penyelesaian tersebut tunggal. ■</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark69"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark70"></a>3. MODEL JARINGAN ANTRIAN FORK-JOIN TAKSIKLIK</span></h6>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Dengan notasi aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus</span><span class="font49"> persamaan (1) dan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(2) dapat dituliskan sebagai berikut</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ik</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ik</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50">-</span><span class="font49">1)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) =</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font58">© </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">), jika </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font50">≠ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">φ</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>j</sup> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">P(i)</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49">, &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;,jika </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font50">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">φ</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Pengertian tentang jaringan antrian </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">fork-joint </span><span class="font49">berikut mengikuti dalam Krivulin (2000). Diperhatikan suatu jaringan dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> titik pelayan tunggal (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">single-server</span><span class="font49">) dan pelanggan kelas tunggal (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">single-class</span><span class="font49">). Struktur jaringan antrian ini dapat dinyatakan dengan graf berarah taksiklik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> = (</span><span class="font36">N, A</span><span class="font49">) dengan busur yang ditentukan oleh rute transisi pelanggan. Untuk setiap titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font36">N</span><span class="font49">, didefinisikan himpunan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">pendahulu</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">predecessors</span><span class="font49">) dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">penerus </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">successors</span><span class="font49">) titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> berturut-turut dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) = { </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font50"> | </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font36">A </span><span class="font49">) dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) = { </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font50"> | </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font36">A </span><span class="font49">).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Untuk setiap titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font36">N </span><span class="font49">terdiri dari sebuah pelayan dan penyangga dengan kapasitas takhingga yang bekerja dengan prinsip </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">First-In First-Out </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">FIFO</span><span class="font49">). Pada waktu-awal jaringan bekerja diasumsikan bahwa pelayan bebas pelanggan, penyangga untuk semua titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font50">≠ </span><span class="font26">∅</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">dalam keadaan kosong, sedangkan penyangga titik yang tidak mempunyai pendahulu (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font26">∅</span><span class="font49">) mempunyai takhingga banyak pelanggan.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Operasi </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">fork</span><span class="font49"> pada titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> diawali setiap kali layanan sebuah pelanggan selesai dan diperoleh beberapa pelanggan baru untuk antrian berikutnya. Banyaknya pelanggan baru yang muncul pada titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i </span><span class="font49">sebanyak titik dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">). Pelanggan-pelanggan baru ini secara serentak meninggalkan titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> dan menuju titik-titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) secara terpisah. Operasi </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">join</span><span class="font49"> pada titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> terjadi saat pelanggan-pelanggan datang ke titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> , tidak hanya di menunggu di penyangga, tetapi juga menunggu sedikitnya satu pelanggan dari setiap titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">∈</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) datang. Segera setelah pelanggan datang, bersama satu pelanggan dari setiap titik pendahulunya, mereka bersatu menjadi satu pelanggan dan masuk dalam penyangga dalam pelayan berikutnya. Dalam pengoperasian jaringan ini diasumsikan bahwa perpindahan pelanggan antar titik tidak memerlukan waktu.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = [ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">1</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) , </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">2</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">), ... , </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)]</span><span class="font45"><sup>T</sup> </span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">1</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) , </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">2</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">), ... , </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)]</span><span class="font45"><sup>T</sup> </span><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(3)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">(4)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = [</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> =</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span></p>
