<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">t</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">nk</span><span class="font50"> _</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Persamaan (3) dan (4) di atas</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">menjadi</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dapat dituliskan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> -</span><span class="font49">1).</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">),</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> yang unsur-unsur adalah</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ij</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font19"><sup>,</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50">0, jika </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50">) ; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font50">, untuk yang lain.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(5)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">(6)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Perhatikan bahwa </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> merupakan matriks</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">kedampingan dari graf stuktur jaringan antrian. Dari persamaan (5) dan (6) dapat dituliskan persamaan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> -</span><span class="font49">1). &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(7)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Teorema 6. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Diberikan jaringan antrian fork-join tak siklik dengan graf struktur jaringannya yang mempunyai panjang lintasan terpanjang p dan matriks kedampingan G. Persamaan keadaan eksplisit jaringan tersebut adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">= A</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">1</span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font49"> (8) </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">dengan A</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">=</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>p</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) menyatakan waktu kedatangan pelanggan ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> pada titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) menyatakan waktu keberangkatan pelanggan ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> pada titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">, dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ik </span><span class="font49">menyatakan lama waktu layanan untuk pelanggan ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> pada pelayan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">. Diasumsikan jaringan mulai beroperasi pada nol waktu, yaitu bahwa </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(0) = 0 dan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<h6><a name="bookmark71"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark72"></a>Bukti:</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Dari hasil pada persamaan (7) dapat dituliskan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> -</span><span class="font49">1)). Karena </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49"> adalah matriks kedampingan graf taksiklik dengan panjang lintasan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49">, maka menurut Lema 4, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>q</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> = </span><span class="font9" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> untuk semua </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font50"> &gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49">. Akibatnya (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>k</sub></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>q</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> = </span><span class="font9" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> untuk semua </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font50"> &gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49">. Selanjutnya menurut Lema 5, persamaan ini mempunyai penyelesaian</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>p</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> -</span><span class="font49">1))</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">= ((</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>p</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> -</span><span class="font49">1)).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">■</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<h6><a name="bookmark73"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark74"></a>Contoh 1.</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Jaringan antrian </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">fork-join</span><span class="font49"> taksiklik dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> = 5 diperlihatkan dalam Gambar 1 berikut.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> untuk semua </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">0, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> = 1, ..., </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n.</span><span class="font49"> Dinamika</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">antrian pada titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> dapat dinyatakan dengan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = max(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ik</span><span class="font49"> + </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">), </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ik</span><span class="font49"> + </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font49"> 1)) ,</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>

<p><span class="font49">Nampak bahwa panjang lintasan terpanjangnya adalah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49"> = 2. Dari persamaan (8) diperoleh persamaan keadaan</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> -</span><span class="font49">1) , dengan</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">= (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊕</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span></p>

<h6><a name="bookmark75"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark76"></a>4. EVALUASI KINERJA JARINGAN ANTRIAN</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Diperhatikan waktu penuntasan siklus layanan jaringan sebagai barisan siklus layanan: siklus kepertama mulai saat waktu awal, dan berakhir segera setelah semua pelayan dalam jaringan menuntaskan layanan kepertamanya, siklus kedua berakhir segera setelah semua pelayan dalam jaringan menuntaskan layanan keduanya, dan seterusnya. Dengan demikan waktu penuntasan siklus ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> pada titik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> adalah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) , sehingga waktu penuntasan siklus ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> pada jaringan dapat dinyatakan sebagai</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">max</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49">(0) = 0, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> = 1, ..., </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> = 0, 1, 2, ....</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya waktu siklus layanan jaringan dapat dinyatakan dengan:</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">γ </span><span class="font49">= lim max(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)) .</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">→∞ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark77"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark78"></a>Contoh 2:</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Dari hasil dalam Contoh 1 pada Tabel 1 nampak bahwa waktu penuntasan siklus ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> dari jaringan tersebut adalah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50"><sub>5</sub></span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">). Perhitungan secara numerik mengenai </span><span class="font50">γ </span><span class="font49">dari Contoh 1, diperoleh hasil seperti dalam Tabel 2 berikut.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Nampak dalam contoh ini bahwa nilai</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">γ </span><span class="font49">= lim max(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)) </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">→∞ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">= lim </span><span class="font49" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50"><sub>5</sub></span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)) = 5. </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">→∞ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Dengan menggunakan program Matlab dapat ditentukan bahwa eigennilai aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus </span><span class="font49">maksimum matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> adalah </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) = 5 dan eigenvektor yang bersesuaian adalah </span><span class="font10">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε ε</span><span class="font49"> 0 </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> 3</span><span class="font10">]</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>T</sup></span><span class="font49"> .</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Secara umum sifat yang muncul pada contoh-contoh di atas diberikan dalam teorema berikut ini.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Teorema 7. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Jaringan antrian fork-join taksiklik kapasitas penyangga takhingga, dengan persamaan keadaan eksplisit jaringan tersebut adalah </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">(k) =</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A(k) </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">⊗</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">(k </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">1), k = 1, 2, ..., mempunyai waktu penuntasan siklus layanan</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">γ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">=</span><span class="font49"> lim </span><span class="font49" style="text-decoration:underline;">1</span><span class="font49"> max(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)) </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)), </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">→∞ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">yaitu eigennilai max-plus maksimum matriks A(k) tersebut.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark79"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark80"></a>Bukti:</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Perhatikan bahwa</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50"> -</span><span class="font49">1)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">= (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k-</span><span class="font49">1)</span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">… </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(2) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(1)) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(0).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Karena dalam tulisan ini diasumsikan bahwa</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(1) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(2) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">...</span><span class="font49"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(0) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">0</span><span class="font49">, maka </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">0 </span><span class="font49">, sehingga </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = ma</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>j</sub></span><span class="font49">x [(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>ij</sub></span><span class="font49">]</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">max</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = max { max [( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>ij</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> )</span><span class="font49">]}. </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ij</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Bobot rata-rata maksimum sirkuit elementer dalam graf presede</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>n</sub></span><span class="font49">n matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> tersebut </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) = </span><span class="font42">⊕</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font50">(1/</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">trace(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49">) ) , </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font45">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya diperoleh bahwa</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) =max [(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49">) ] = max (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k </sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>j</sub> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ij </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>j</sub></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">sehingga</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">max</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">) = max (max ( (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50"><sub>max</sub> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ij</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">=(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49"> .</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Dengan demikian diperoleh bahwa</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">γ </span><span class="font49">= lim max(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)) </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">→∞ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">= lim </span><span class="font49" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">→∞ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">= </span><span class="font49">lim<sup>1</sup> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">)) </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">). </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46">→∞ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font48">■</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">yang merupakan eigennilai aljabar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">max-plus </span><span class="font49">maksimum matriks </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">. Oleh karena itu berlaku</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="font49">= (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> </span><span class="font49">,</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">untuk suatu eigenvektor </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="font49">. Hal ini berakibat ma</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>j</sub></span><span class="font49">x((</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>ij</sub></span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="font49">) = (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50"><sub>max</sub></span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">))</span><span class="font27"><sup>⊗</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font49">ma</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>j</sub></span><span class="font49">x(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">v<sup>*</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>j</sub></span><span class="font49">) , dengan max (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">v<sup>*</sup></span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font50">≠ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ε</span><span class="font49"> . Vektor </span><span class="font50">- </span><span class="font49">max (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">v<sup>*</sup></span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> </span><span class="font49">juga </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>j</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>j</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">merupakan eigenvektor yang berkaitan dengan eigenvektor </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font45">max</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49">) di atas, dengan</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font50">- </span><span class="font49">max (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">v<sup>*</sup></span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font26">⊗</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font49">max (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">v<sup>*</sup></span><span class="font49"> ) = 0.</span></p></li></ul>
