<h6><a name="bookmark83"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark84"></a>BEBERAPA SIFAT IDEAL GELANGGANG POLINOM MIRING: SUATU KAJIAN PUSTAKA</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">AMIR KAMAL AMIR</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Jurusan Matematika, FMIPA, Universitas Hasanuddin 90245 Email : </span><a href="mailto:amirkamalamir@yahoo.com"><span class="font49">amirkamalamir@yahoo.com</span></a></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark85"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark86"></a>INTISARI</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">Misalkan </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font48"> adalah suatu gelanggang dengan elemen satuan 1, </span><span class="font8" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48"> adalah suatu endomorfisme, dan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">δ </span><span class="font48">adalah suatu </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ —</span><span class="font48"> derivatif. Gelanggang polinom miring (</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">skew polynomial</span><span class="font48">) atas </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font48"> dengan variabel </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x </span><span class="font48">adalah gelanggang: </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x;</span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">,δ]</span><span class="font26"> = </span><span class="font48">{</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48"> (</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48">) </span><span class="font26">= </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">a<sub>n</sub>x<sup>n</sup></span><span class="font26"> + —+ </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font48">0 | </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">ai</span><span class="font26"> ∈ </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font48">} dengan aturan perkalian </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">xa</span><span class="font26"> = </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48">(</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font48">)</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font26"> + </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">(a</span><span class="font48">) . Penelitian ini akan mengidentifikasi ideal-ideal dari gelanggang polinom miring dalam hal </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font26"> = </span><span class="font48">0</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">.</span><span class="font48"> Lebih jelasnya, akan didentifikasi hal-hal berikut: (1) ideal dari gelanggang polinom miring </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48">; </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48">]; (2) ideal prim dari gelanggang polinom miring </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48">; </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48">]; dan ideal </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48"> — prim dari gelanggang polinom miring </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48">; </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48">].</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Kata kunci: automorfisme, daerah integral, </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font26"> — </span><span class="font48">prim.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark87"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark88"></a>SOME IDEAL PROPERTIES OF</span><br><br><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark89"></a>SKEW POLYNOMIAL RING: A LITERATURE STUDY</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">AMIR KAMAL AMIR</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Mathematics Department, FMIPA, Hasanuddin University 90245 Email : </span><a href="mailto:amirkamalamir@yahoo.com"><span class="font49">amirkamalamir@yahoo.com</span></a></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark90"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark91"></a>ABSTRACT</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">Let R be a ring with identity 1 and </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48"> be an endomorphism of </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font48"> and </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font48"> be a left </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48"> — derivation. The skew polynomial ring over </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font48"> in an indeterminate </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48"> is: </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48">; </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48">, </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">]</span><span class="font26"> = </span><span class="font48">{</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48"> (</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48">) </span><span class="font26">= </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">a<sub>n</sub>x<sup>n</sup></span><span class="font26"> +-----+ </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font48">0 | </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">ai </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">∈ </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font48">} with </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">xa</span><span class="font26"> = </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48">(</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font48">)</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font26"> + </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font48">(</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font48">) The aim of this research is to investigate the ideals in the above skew polynomial ring in case of </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font26"> = </span><span class="font48">0 . Precisely, we will investigate the following: (1) the ideal of skew polynomial ring </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48">;</span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48">]; (2) the ideal prim of skew polynomial ring </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48">;</span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48">]; and (3) the </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font26"> — </span><span class="font48">prim ideal of skew polynomial ring </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font48">[</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48">; </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48">].</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Keywords: automorphism, integral area, </span><span class="font26" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font26"> — </span><span class="font48">prim.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark92"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark93"></a>1. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PENDAHULUAN</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Definisi dari gelanggang polinom miring (gelanggang takkomutatif) ini pertama kali diperkenalkan oleh Ore (1993) yang mengombinasikan ide awal dari Hilbert (kasus </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">0</span><span class="font49">) dan Schlessinger (kasus </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">1</span><span class="font49">). Sejak kemunculan artikel dari Ore ini, gelanggang polinom miring telah memerankan peran yang penting dalam teori gelanggang takkomutatif dan telah banyak peneliti yang bergelut dalam teori gelanggang takkomutatif menginvestigasi bentuk gelanggang tersebut dari berbagai sudut pandang, seperti teori ideal, teori order, teori Galois, dan aljabar homologi.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Berikut diberikan definisi lengkap dari gelanggang polinom miring.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Definisi 1. </span><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> adalah suatu gelanggang dengan identitas 1, </span><span class="font8" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font49"> adalah suatu endomorfisme dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R,</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font49"> adalah suatu </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ —</span><span class="font50"> derivatif</span><span class="font49">, yaitu:</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49">(i) . </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font49"> adalah suatu endomorfisme pada </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R, </span><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> sebagai grup penjumlahan</span></p></li>
<li>
<p><span class="font49">(ii) . </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">(ab</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">(b</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49"> untuk setiap</span></p></li></ul>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b </span><span class="font27" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font50">.</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Gelanggang polinom miring atas </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> dengan variabel </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x </span><span class="font49">adalah gelanggang:</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R[x;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">=</span><span class="font50"> {</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a<sub>n</sub>x<sup>n</sup></span><span class="font51"> + -L + </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font48">0 </span><span class="font50">| </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font50"> } </span><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">xa</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> ) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50">( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> ), </span><span class="font51">V </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a </span><span class="font27" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> .</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Suatu elemen </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49"> dari gelanggang polinom miring </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">mempunyai bentuk kanonik</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">r</span></p>
<h4><a name="bookmark94"></a><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><a name="bookmark95"></a>p </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">= </span><span class="font58" style="font-style:italic;">∑ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">ix<sup>i</sup></span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">r</span><span class="font27" style="font-variant:small-caps;">∈</span><span class="font27" style="font-weight:bold;font-variant:small-caps;">Z</span><span class="font27" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sub>+</sub>=</span><span class="font50" style="font-variant:small-caps;">{0,1,</span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font50" style="font-variant:small-caps;">}, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i </span><span class="font27" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font27" style="font-variant:small-caps;">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-variant:small-caps;">1,</span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font50" style="font-variant:small-caps;">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">r</span><span class="font50">. </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font36">=</span><span class="font48">0</span></h4>
<p><span class="font49">Apabila </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">1 </span><span class="font49">atau </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font49"> adalah suatu endomorfisme identitas, maka gelanggang polinom miring cukup ditulis </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">. Untuk hal </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">O</span><span class="font49">, gelanggang polinom miring cukup ditulis </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">. Sedangkan untuk kasus </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">1 </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">O </span><span class="font49">gelanggang polinom miring cukup ditulis </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">, yang merupakan gelanggang polinom biasa. Dalam tulisan ini gelanggang </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> yang digunakan adalah gelanggang yang merupakan daerah integral komutatif dengan elemen satuan yang selanjutnya disimbolkan dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">D.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Contoh 1. </span><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">C </span><span class="font49">adalah himpunan bilangan kompleks. </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font49"> suatu endomorfisme pada </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">C </span><span class="font49">yang didefinisikan sebagai </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font11">( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">bi</span><span class="font11"> ) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font51">—</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">bi</span><span class="font49">, untuk setiap </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">bi</span><span class="font27" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font56" style="font-style:italic;">C</span><span class="font49"> , dan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">O</span><span class="font49">. Akan ditunjukkan ketidak komutatifan dalam gelanggang polinom miring </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">C </span><span class="font50">[ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> ;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font10">[ </span><span class="font50">(2 </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">3i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font10"> ][ </span><span class="font50">(4</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">5i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font10"> ]</span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(2 </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">3i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font10">[ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> (4</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">5i</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font10">] </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">(2</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">3i)</span><span class="font56" style="font-style:italic;">[</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">(4</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">5i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x </span><span class="font56" style="font-style:italic;">] </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">(2 </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">3i</span><span class="font50">)(4</span><span class="font51">—</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">5i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(23 </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">2i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"><sup>2</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font10">[ </span><span class="font50">(4</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">5i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font10"> ] [ </span><span class="font50">(2</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">3i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font10"> ]</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">(4</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">5i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font10">[ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> (2</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50">3</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font10">] </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">(4</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">5i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font10">[ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">(2</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">3i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font10"> ] </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50">(4</span><span class="font51">+</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">5i</span><span class="font50">)(2</span><span class="font51">—</span><span class="font50">3</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(23</span><span class="font51">—</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">2i</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> <sup>2</sup></span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark96"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark97"></a>2. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;MASALAH DAN PEMBAHASAN</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Masalah yang akan dibahas dalam bagian ini adalah mengidentifikasi bentuk-bentuk ideal dari berbagai bentuk gelanggang polinom miring. Secara mendetail, bentuk-bentuk ideal yang akan diidentifikasi adalah sebagai berikut:</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49">1.i deal dari gelanggang polinom miring </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D[ x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">;</span></p></li>
<li>
<p><span class="font49">2.i deal prim dari gelanggang polinom miring </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font50"> [ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">;</span></p></li>
<li>
<p><span class="font49">3.i deal </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51"> — </span><span class="font50">prim </span><span class="font49">dari gelanggang polinom miring </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50"> ]</span><span class="font49">.</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Sekadar mengingat kembali, berikut ini disajikan definisi dari ideal dan ideal prim.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Definisi 2. </span><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> adalah suatu gelanggang. Suatu himpunan bagian </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> dikatakan suatu ideal kanan dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> jika :</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49">1. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I,+</span><span class="font49">) adalah suatu grup bagian dari (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R,+</span><span class="font49">),</span></p></li>
<li>
<p><span class="font49">2.</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;xr</span><span class="font49"> berada dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> untuk setiap </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49"> dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I </span><span class="font49">dan setiap </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">r</span><span class="font49"> dalam </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49">.</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Suatu ideal kiri dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> didefinisikan serupa dengan ideal kanan. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> dikatakan ideal dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> jika </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I </span><span class="font49">merupakan ideal kanan dan sekaligus ideal kiri dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49">. Selanjutnya suatu ideal </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> dikatakan ideal prim jika dan hanya jika untuk setiap ideal-ideal </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A, B </span><span class="font49">dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"> implikasi berikut bernilai benar: Jika </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">AB</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">⊂</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> , maka </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">⊂</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> atau </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">⊂</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> . Pernyataan terakhir ini ekuivalen dengan: jika </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ab</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49">, maka </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> atau </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark98"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark99"></a>2.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Ideal dari Gelanggang Polinom Miring </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font50"> [ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50">]</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Teorema 1. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Misalkan D adalah suatu daerah integral komutatif yang bukan merupakan lapangan. Jika </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font51"> ≠ </span><span class="font50">1, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">untuk semua bilangan asli n dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">] </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">adalah suatu ideal dari </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">], </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">maka f(x) = x.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark100"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark101"></a>Bukti:</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48">j </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48">l</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f<sub>n</sub>x<sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> ≠ </span><span class="font50">O </span><span class="font49">untuk suatu </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50">{1,2, </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">}</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">(i)</span><span class="font49"> . Akan tunjukkan bahwa </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48"> j </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">O </span><span class="font49">.</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Karena &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">, &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;diperoleh</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">af</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50"> [ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> ;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">], </span><span class="font51">V </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font49">. Oleh karena itu terdapat </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font49"> sedemikian sehingga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">af</span><span class="font50"> ( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> ) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> ( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> ) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b </span><span class="font49">atau</span></p>
<h4><a name="bookmark102"></a><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup><a name="bookmark103"></a>a</sup></span><span class="font19"> (</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>f</sup></span><span class="font48">j</span><span class="font19"><sup>+ </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>f</sup></span><span class="font48">1</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>x</sup></span><span class="font19"><sup> + </sup></span><span class="font0" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>l</sup></span><span class="font19"><sup> + </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>f</sup></span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>x</sup></span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font19">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font19">(</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>f</sup></span><span class="font48">j</span><span class="font19"><sup>+ </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>f</sup></span><span class="font48">1</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>x</sup></span><span class="font19"><sup> + </sup></span><span class="font0" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>l</sup></span><span class="font19"><sup> + </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>f</sup></span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>x</sup></span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font19">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b.</span></h4>
<p><span class="font49">Dari persamaan ini diperoleh </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">af</span><span class="font48">j </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48">j </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">af</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font49">. Karena </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> ≠ </span><span class="font50">O &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">diperoleh</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>i</sup></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font49">, yang mengakibatkan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font51"> ≠ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49"> sehingga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48">j </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-variant:small-caps;">o</span><span class="font49" style="font-variant:small-caps;">.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">(ii)</span><span class="font49"> . Sebagai kosekwensi dari (i), diperoleh </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48">l</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x<sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50">, (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> .</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font50">. </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48"> j </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">O) </span><span class="font49">.</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya akan tunjukkan bahwa </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48">i </span><span class="font51">≠ </span><span class="font50">O.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Andaikan bahwa &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48">i </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">O</span><span class="font49">, &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;maka</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48">2</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x<sup>n</sup></span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-variant:small-caps;">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">].</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Dari sini diperoleh,</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>f</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>f</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font19"> <sup>+</sup> </span><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font19"><sup>+</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> =</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>σ </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>1f</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">)X</span><span class="font19"><sup>+</sup></span><span class="font52">L </span><span class="font19"><sup>+</sup></span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>σ</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">fx</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font27" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>f</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x)D[</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>χ</sup></span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>σ</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∉</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">^<sup>1</sup>(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48">2</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> + ∙∙∙ +</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">&quot;<sup>1</sup>(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x<sup>n</sup></span><span class="font51"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font50"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font26">∉</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D[x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">].</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Hal ini kontradiksi dengan asumsi bahwa </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D[x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">adalah ideal prim.</span></p>

<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">af<sub>t</sub></span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f<sub>t</sub> </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">. Karena </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font51"> ≠ </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f<sub>t</sub> </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">≠</span><span class="font50"> 0 </span><span class="font49">, maka</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font50"><sup> 1</sup> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font49">. Hal ini kontradiksi dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">σ<sup>n</sup></span><span class="font51"> ≠ </span><span class="font50">1 </span><span class="font49">untuk semua bilangan asli </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n.</span></p>

<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Lema 1. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Misalkan</span><span class="font51"> Λ=</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">adalah suatu gelanggang polinom miring dan A adalah ideal dari </span><span class="font51">Λ</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">. </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font51"> ∩ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">{0} </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">j'ika dan hanya j'ika </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">AK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">^</span><span class="font50">]0 </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">, dalam hal ini K adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">lapangan pembagian dari D.</span></p>

Hal ini kontradiksi dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">AK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] 0 </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ff</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">.«</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Teorema 2. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Misalkan P adalah ideal prim minimal dari</span><span class="font51"> Λ=</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">dan K adalah lapangan hasil bagi dari D, maka </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">adalah ideal prim dari </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font50"> [ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark106"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark107"></a>Bukti:</span></h6>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49">(i) . Akan ditunjukkan bahwa </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50"> [ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">ideal.</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">. Untuk membuktikan bahwa </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">adalah ideal , maka akan ditunjukkan bahwa </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50"> [ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50"> [ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">. Karena &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">berarti</span></p>

<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font36">=</span><span class="font48">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">^</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">. Karena </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">^</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">K </span><span class="font49">adalah lapangan hasil bagi dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font49">, maka dapat ditemukan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font51"> ≠ </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font49">sedemikian sehingga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">dh</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">. Selanjutnya, dengan alasan yang sama dapat ditemukan juga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font51"> ≠ </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font49">sedemikian sehingga</span></p>

<p><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>a</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>b</sup></span><span class="font50"><sup> (</sup>.</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">.</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>h</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x)</span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font45"><sup>(</sup>.</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">.</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font45"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>x</sup></span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">, karena </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49">(ii) . Akan ditunjukkan bahwa </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">prim</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Untuk menunjukkan hal ini, akan ditunjukkan bahwa jika &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">, maka</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">atau </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Karena &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">, maka dapat</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dimisalkan &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font58">∑ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">, dengan</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font36">=</span><span class="font48">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">untuk suatu </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font49">bilangan asli. Karena </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font49"> adalah lapangan hasil bagi dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">D,</span><span class="font49"> maka untuk setiap </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> terdapat </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D </span><span class="font49">sedemikian sehingga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d<sub>i</sub>k<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">. Oleh karena itu, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d<sub>i</sub>k<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> karena P adalah ideal prim dari </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">. Dari sini sudah dapat disimpulkan bahwa terdapat </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font51">≠ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font49"> sedemikian sehingga</span></p>

<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya, andaikan &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∉</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">PK</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">dan</span></p>

Mengingat </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> ideal prim, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">dg</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> , dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∉</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> , maka </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font49"> yang berarti bahwa </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font51"> ∩ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">{0} </span><span class="font49">. Hal ini kontradiksi dengan Lema 1. ■</span></p>

<h6><a name="bookmark108"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark109"></a>2.2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Ideal </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">prim </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">dari Gelanggang Polinom Miring </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50"> , </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50">]</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Definisi 3. </span><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49">adalah suatu gelangang polinom miring. Suatu </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ideal</span><span class="font49"> dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> . </span><span class="font49">Suatu </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" Dalam kasus 0 adalah suatu </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">prim</span><span class="font49"> ideal dari </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49">, dikatakan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">R </span><span class="font49">adalah suatu gelanggang </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">prim</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> .</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Teorema 3. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Misalkan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">adalah suatu automorfisme dari gelanggang R, dan misalkan I adalah suatu ideal murni dari R sedemikian sehingga </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font50">. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">adalah </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">prime </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">jika dan hanya jika untuk sembarang </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">terdapat </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">Z </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">sedemikain sehingga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ab</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∉</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> .</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark110"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark111"></a>Bukti:</span></h6>

<p><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">A, C</span><span class="font49"> adalah </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ideal</span><span class="font49"> yang tidak berada dalam ideal </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49">. <p><span class="font49">Kasus 1. Jika </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font50">0, </span><span class="font49">maka </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">C</span><span class="font49"> sehingga dari </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ab</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∉</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> diperoleh </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">AC</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">⊄</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> .</span></p>
