style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font49"> sehingga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">AC</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">⊄</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> .</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Dari kasus 1 dan 2 disimpulkan bahwa </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> adalah suatu ideal </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">prime</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> .</span></p>
<h4><a name="bookmark114"></a><span class="font27"><a name="bookmark115"></a>⇒</span></h4>
<p><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> adalah </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">prime</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font50">. </span><span class="font49">Himpunan-himpunan</span></p>
<p><span class="font36">∞</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font58">∑ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R<sub>σ</sub><sup>i</sup></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">r</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font36">=</span><span class="font48">0</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font36">∞</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">C</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font58">∑ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font36">=</span><span class="font48">0</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">adalah </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">ideal</span><span class="font49"> yang tidak berada dalam ideal </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49">, sehingga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">AC</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">⊄</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> .</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Konsekuensinya, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>i</sup></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>j</sup></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∉</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> untuk suatu </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font50">0, </span><span class="font49">sehingga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>i</sup></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b)</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font51"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>i</sup></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font27">∉</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font50">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">Teorema 4. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Misalkan M adalah suatu idel maksimal dari </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">; </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">] </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font51"> ∩ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font51"> ≠ </span><span class="font50">{0} </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Jika </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∉</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">, maka </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font51"> ∩ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">adalah suatu ideal </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">prime</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">.</span></p>

<h6><a name="bookmark122"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark123"></a>DAFTAR PUSTAKA</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Ore, O. 1933.Theory of Non-Commutative Polynomials. </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Annals of Mathematics</span><span class="font49">. </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">34: </span><span class="font49">480—508.</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">UJI KENORMALAN UNIVARIAT: SUATU KAJIAN PUSTAKA</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">I WAYAN SUMARJAYA</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Jurusan Matematika, FMIPA, Universitas Udayana Email: </span><a href="mailto:sumarjaya@unud.ac.id"><span class="font49">sumarjaya@unud.ac.id</span></a></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark124"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark125"></a>INTISARI</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">Sebagian besar prosedur statistika terutama inferensi statistika mengasumsikan distribusi sampel adalah normal. Asumsi kenormalan ini harus diuji untuk menjamin penggunaan statistik uji yang benar dan sesuai, sehingga nantinya diperoleh simpulan yang sahih. Penelitian ini membahas perkembangan uji-uji kenormalan univariat: uji berdasarkan fungsi distribusi empiris, uji berdasarkan momen, uji berdasarkan korelasi atau regresi, uji berdasarkan entropi sampel, uji berdasarkan metode kernel, uji berdasarkan karakteristik Polya, dan uji berdasarkan metode nonparametrik. Penelitian ini juga membahas uji kenormalan yang mampu mendeteksi pencilan dan uji omnibus yang mampu memberikan informasi tambahan tentang ketidaknormalan. sdfsdllflsdflskdflsklfkslfksdllskflskflsllsdfs</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Kata kunci: uji kenormalan univariat, uji kenormalan omnibus.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark126"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark127"></a>UNIVARIATE NORMALITY TEST: A LITERATURE STUDY</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">I WAYAN SUMARJAYA</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Mathematics Department, FMIPA, Udayana University Email: </span><a href="mailto:sumarjaya@unud.ac.id"><span class="font49">sumarjaya@unud.ac.id</span></a></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark128"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark129"></a>ABSTRACT</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">Almost all statistical procedures, especially statistical inference, assumed that the sample distribution is normally distributed. This normality assumption must be tested to ensure the correct use of the test statistic, hence resulting a correct conclusion. This research discusses some univariate normality tests: test based on empirical distribution function, test based on moments, test based on correlation or regression, test based on sample entropy, test based on kernel method, test based on Polya characteristics, and test based on nonparametric method. This research also discuss normality test that capable of detecting outliers and discuss omnibus test that can give additional information about nonnormality.</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Keywords: univariate normality test, omnibus normality test.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark130"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark131"></a>1. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PENDAHULUAN</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Sebagian besar prosedur statistika terutama inferensi statistika mengasumsikan distribusi sampel adalah normal. Asumsi kenormalan ini perlu diuji untuk menjamin penggunaan statistik uji yang benar dan sesuai, sehingga nantinya diperoleh simpulan yang sahih, misalnya pada bidang kesehatan (lihat Lumley, 2002)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Secara umum, uji kenormalan dapat dikelompokkan ke dalam beberapa kategori: uji berdasarkan fungsi distribusi empiris, uji berdasarkan momen, uji berdasarkan korelasi atau regresi, uji berdasarkan entropi, uji berdasarkan karakteristik Polya, uji berdasarkan metode kernel, dan uji berdasarkan metode nonparametrik.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Studi komprehensif perbandingan uji-uji kenormalan telah dilakukan antara lain oleh Stephens (1972), Koziol (1986), Dufour </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49">(1998), Seier (2002), Coin dan Corradetti (2006), Farrell dan Rogers-Stewart (2006), Yazici dan Yolacan (2007), Tanweer-ul-Islam (2008), Breton </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (2008), dan Tanweer-ul-Islam dan Zaman (2008).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Penelitian ini juga membahas uji kenormalan yang mampu mendeteksi pencilan dan uji omnibus yang mampu memberikan informasi tambahan tentang ketidaknormalan distribusi alternatif.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">2. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;METODE-METODE UJI KENORMALAN</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">UNIVARIAT</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Uji tentang kenormalan dimulai pada awal 1900 oleh Karl Pearson (lihat Yazici dan Yolacan, 2007). Selanjutnya beberapa dekade setelah itu banyak peneliti mengembangkan statistik uji untuk uji kenormalan.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark132"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark133"></a>2.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Uji Kenormalan Berdasarkan Fungsi Distribusi Empiris</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Uji fungsi distribusi empiris, disebut pula uji jarak (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">distance test</span><span class="font49">), berdasarkan perbandingan antara fungsi distribusi empiris </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">F</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i / n</span><span class="font49"> dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">distribusi hipotesis di bawah kenormalan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Z<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> yang biasanya didefinisikan sebagai</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">Z<sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">=φ{ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x &nbsp;&nbsp;x</span><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"> ^ &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(1)</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font6">k </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:line-through;">x</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49"> masing-masing menyatakan rata-rata sampel dan simpangan baku sampel (lihat Dufour, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> 1998; Lee, 1998). Secara umum uji fungsi distribusi empiris terbagi atas dua kelompok (Lee, 1998). Pertama, uji yang melibatkan supremum seperti uji Kolmogorov-Smirnov. Kedua, uji yang menghitung kuadrat perbedaan seperti uji Cramér-von Mises. Berikut akan diberikan uji-uji yang termasuk ke dalam kedua kelompok tersebut beserta modifikasinya.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Cramér (1928) mengusulkan statistik uji</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">VM </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font57">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font2">=</span><span class="font45">i </span><span class="font49">[</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z‘</span><span class="font6"> - </span><span class="font49">(2</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6"> — </span><span class="font49">1)/2</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">]</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font6">+</span><span class="font49"><sup>1</sup> /(<sup>1</sup>2</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">), (2)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z<sub>i</sub> </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">=</span><span class="font6"> Φ</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">e;<sub>in</sub></span><span class="font49"> / </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">=</span><span class="font49"> 1, </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">k</span><span class="font49"> , </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">; </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">e:<sub>in</sub></span><span class="font49"> adalah statistik terurut sisaan dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font18">[</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">- </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font2">~</span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font57">∑</span><span class="font2">&quot;=</span><span class="font49"><sub>ι</sub> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font18">] </span><span class="font45"><sup>1/2</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">. </span><span class="font49">Statistik uji (2) disebut pula statistik uji Cramér-von Mises. Selanjutnya, Watson (lihat Stephens, 1972) memodifikasi statistik Cramér-von Mises pada persamaan (2) dan mengusulkan statistik</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">W </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49">VM</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font6">- </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font49">1/2)</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font49">, (3)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49">(1/ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font57" style="text-decoration:underline;">∑</span><span class="font49">&quot;=<sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Uji fungsi distribusi empiris selanjutnya diusulkan oleh Kolmogorov (1933) dengan statistik uji berikut:</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">D</span><span class="font45"><sup>+</sup> </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49">max[(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> / </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font6">- </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> ], 1 </span><span class="font6">≤ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6"> ≤ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">;</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">D</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup> </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49">max[ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font49">1)/ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> ], 1 </span><span class="font6">≤ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6"> ≤ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<sup>(4)</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">D </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49">max( </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font45"><sup>+</sup>, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">D</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup> </span><span class="font49">);</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z</span><span class="font49">ˆ</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> menyatakan distribusi normal standar dan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> menyatakan jumlah sampel. Nilai-nilai kritis untuk uji Kolmogorov-Smirnov dapat dilihat pada Kolmogorov (1933).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Kemudian Anderson dan Darling (1952, 1954) mengusulkan statistik uji</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">AD </span><span class="font6">= - </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font45"><sup>-1</sup> </span><span class="font57">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font2">=</span><span class="font49"><sub>1</sub>(2 </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6">-</span><span class="font49">1)[ln </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">+</span><span class="font49"> ln(1 </span><span class="font6">- </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> ^)] </span><span class="font6">- </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">, (5) dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">z<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> menyatakan peluang normal standar (lihat juga Yacizi dan Yolacan, 2007; Stephens, 1972; dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Dufour </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> ,1998). Hipotesis nul akan ditolak apabila statistik uji (5) lebih dari 2,492 (lihat Yazici dan Yolacan, 2007).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Ajne (1968) mengusulkan statistik uji</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">AJ</span><span class="font6">=</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> /4)</span><span class="font7"><sup>-</sup> </span><span class="font49">(<sup>2</sup>/ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> )</span><span class="font57">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font2">=</span><span class="font49"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font57">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font2">=</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">m <sub>ιj</sub></span><span class="font49"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(<sup>6</sup>)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan nilai </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>j</sub></span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font6"> -</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">, jika &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">χ<sub>j</sub></span><span class="font6"> -</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6"> ≤ </span><span class="font49">1/2;</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>j</sub></span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49">1 </span><span class="font6">-</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x<sub>j</sub></span><span class="font6"> -</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;jika &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">χ<sub>j</sub></span><span class="font6"> -</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">&gt;</span><span class="font49">&nbsp;1/2 </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya akan dibahas beberapa modifikasi terhadap statistik Kolmogorov-Smirnov.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">2.1.1 Beberapa modifikasi terhadap statistik Kolmogorov-Smirnov dan Lilliefors</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Kuiper (1962) memodifikasi statistik Kolmogorov-Smirnov pada persamaan (4), dengan statistik</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">V </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49">D</span><span class="font45"><sup>+</sup> </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">D</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font49">. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(7)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya modifikasi terhadap statistik Kuiper pada persamaan (7) dilakukan oleh Stephens (1970) dengan mengusulkan statistik</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">V* </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49">V( </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"><sup>1/2</sup> </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">0,155 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">0,24</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> &quot;<sup>1/2</sup>). &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(8)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Untuk menolak hipotesis nol, statistik uji pada persamaan (8) dibandingkan dengan 1,747 (lihat Yazici dan Yolacan, 2007).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Lilliefors (1967) mengamati bahwa jika satu atau lebih parameter harus diestimasi maka uji tabel standar Kolmogorov-Smirnov tidak lagi berlaku. Selanjutnya Lilliefors (1967) mengusulkan statistik uji</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">D</span><span class="font45">* </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49">max| </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">F</span><span class="font49">*(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font6">- </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49">) |, &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(9)</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">x</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">F</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> </span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49">) menyatakan fungsi distribusi normal kumulatif dengan nilai tengah </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">μ</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49"> serta varians </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">menyatakan fungsi distribusi kumulatif sampel. Secara paralel van Soest juga memodifikasi statistik Kolmogorov-Smirnov (lihat Molin dan Abdi, 1998; Abdi dan Molin, 2007). Modifikasi lain statistik uji Kolmogorov-Smirnov dilakukan oleh Stephens (1970) dengan statistik</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">V* </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49">D( </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"><sup>1/2</sup> </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">0,12 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">0,11 </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> &quot;<sup>1/2</sup>), &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(10)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan D menyatakan statistik Kolmogorov-Smirnov. Untuk menolak hipotesis nol nilai pada persamaan (10) dibandingkan dengan 1,358 (lihat Yazici dan Yolacan, 2007).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Drezner </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (2008) juga memodifikasi statistik Kolmogorov-Smirnov dan mengusulkan statistik </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">D(</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">μ</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">)</span><span class="font49"> dengan vektor </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">μ</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">adalah solusi yang meminimunkan masalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">min[ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D (</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">μ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">)], &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(11)</span></p>
<p><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">μ</span><span class="font45">,</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D (</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">μ</span><span class="font45"> <sup>,</sup></span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">max</span><span class="font31">[</span><span class="font43" style="font-style:italic;">n-</span><span class="font19"><sup>- φ</sup></span><span class="font16">(</span><span class="font43" style="font-style:italic;">'F</span><span class="font16"> J </span><span class="font19"><sup>φ</sup></span><span class="font16">(</span><span class="font43" style="font-style:italic;">'F</span><span class="font16">)</span><span class="font19"><sup>- </sup></span><span class="font43" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font16">1 </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font46"> ≤ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font46"> ≤ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Nilai-nilai kritis untuk statistik (11) dapat dilihat pada Drezner </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (2008).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Arcones dan Wang (2005) mengusulkan perbaikan terhadap statistik uji Lilliefors dengan mengenalkan dua uji berdasarkan proses-U, yaitu </span><span class="font50">~</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">statistik </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>,</sub></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font49"> dan statistik </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>,</sub></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>m</sub></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"> . </span><span class="font49">Statistik </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>,</sub></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>m </sub></span><span class="font49">didefinisikan sebagai</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>

<p><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font49">(12)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font45"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font43"> 1, </span><span class="font33">K</span><span class="font45">,</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>i</sup></span><span class="font43" style="font-style:italic;">m </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">)</span><span class="font39" style="font-style:italic;">∈</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;"> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font43" style="font-style:italic;">m</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan nilai &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d * </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>n</sub>^m</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>l12</sup></span><span class="font58"> ∑ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X<sub>ij</sub></span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>-</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> ) </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;"><sup>,</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dari distribusi </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">N</span><span class="font50">(0,1) </span><span class="font49">adalah 0 dan 3. Konsep momen ini dimunculkan pertama kali oleh Karl Pearson. Selanjutnya, momen ketiga disebut kepencongan (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">skewness</span><span class="font49">) dan momen keempat disebut kurtosis. Dengan demikian penyimpangan dari kenormalan dapat diketahui dari nilai momen-momen yang diduga menggunakan sampel, yakni koefisien kepencongan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">dan koefisien kurtosis</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>

</div><br clear="all">

<p><span class="font45">(</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45"><sub>1,</sub> </span><span class="font33">K</span><span class="font45">,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i<sub>m</sub></span><span class="font45"> )</span><span class="font39">∈</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">I<sub>m</sub></span></p>

<p><span class="font49">dengan nilai </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font58"> <sup>1/2</sup> ∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font51"> — </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">dan nilai</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d ** </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font58"> <sup>1</sup>∑ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">1</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">— </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">. </span><span class="font49">Untuk statistik uji</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dan kurtosis dapat diukur dengan lebih dari satu cara. Salah satu ukuran kurtosis diusulkan oleh Geary (1947). Untuk pembahasan lebih lanjut tentang kepencongan dan kurtosis lihat DeCarlo (1997) dan Doric </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al</span><span class="font49">. (2009).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Uji-uji berdasarkan momen biasanya bersifat omnibus, artinya mampu memberikan informasi tambahan tentang ketidaknormalan distribusi alternatif melalui nilai kepencongan dan kurtosis (lihat Poitras, 2006).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Uji berdasarkan momen pertama kali diusulkan oleh Geary (1947) dengan statistik uji</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">persamaan (13), hipotesis nol akan ditolak apabila</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">~</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D<sub>n</sub> &gt;C <sup>c</sup><sub>ntna</sub></span><span class="font49"> dengan </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font45"> , </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">im &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;n</span><span class="font45"> , </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">im</span><span class="font45">,</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c.</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">rn</span><span class="font45">,</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">„</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">ιnf{</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font50">0: </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P</span><span class="font46">φ</span><span class="font50">{</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">D,,</span><span class="font45">,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font51"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">}</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font50">1 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">}</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">. </span><span class="font49">(14)</span></p>

<p><span class="font49">(20)</span></p>

<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">2.1.2 Beberapa Modifikasi Terhadap Statistik Ajne</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Stephens (1970) memodifikasi statistik yang diusulkan Ajne dengan statistik</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">AJ</span><span class="font45">* </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49">[AJ </span><span class="font6">- </span><span class="font49">(0,7/ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">(0,9 / </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> <sup>2</sup>)][1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">(1,23 / </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">)]. (15) Selanjutnya untuk menolak hipotesis nol statistik uji ini dibandingkan dengan 0,656 (lihat Yazici dan Yolacan, 2007).</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:line-through;">x</span><span class="font49"> menyatakan rata-rata sampel dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c</span><span class="font49"> adalah bilangan real taknegatif.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">D’Agostino dan Pearson mengusulkan statistik uji menggunakan momen Pearson (lihat D’Agostino </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al</span><span class="font49">., 1990)</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">K</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">Z</span><span class="font49"><sup>2</sup> (√</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font45">T</span><span class="font49">)</span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font55" style="font-style:italic;">Z<sup>2</sup> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font11">)</span><span class="font49">, &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(21)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">yang berdistribusi </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">χ</span><span class="font45"> <sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50">(2)</span><span class="font49">. Pada persamaan (21) nilai </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">Z</span><span class="font50"><sup>2</sup> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">&quot;Jb</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">Z</span><span class="font11"><sup>2</sup> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"> <sub>2</sub></span><span class="font11">) </span><span class="font49">adalah pendekatan-pendekatan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">normal terhadap </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">2.2 Uji Kenormalan Berdasarkan Momen</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Konsep uji berdasarkan momen adalah bahwa momen ketiga dan momen keempat yang diberikan oleh</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Pendekatan pengujian menggunakan kepencongan &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">dan kurtosis </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font49">juga diusulkan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">oleh Jarque dan Bera (1980, 1987) dan Bera dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Jarque (1981) dengan statistik uji</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">E</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">X</span><span class="font51" style="text-decoration:underline;"> - </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">μ</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">)</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>3</sup></span><span class="font45"> &nbsp;</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">_ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">E</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">X</span><span class="font51" style="text-decoration:underline;"> - </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">μ</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">)</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>2</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">^</span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font45"><sup>3/2</sup> </span><span class="font51">= &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">σ<sup>3</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(16)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50">JB </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50">W </span><span class="font7"><sub>+</sub> </span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">b</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;">2 </span><span class="font51" style="text-decoration:underline;">- </span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">3)</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>2</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font50">6 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;24</span></p>

<p><span class="font49">(22)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Statistik JB secara asimtotis berdistribusi </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">χ</span><span class="font50"><sup>2</sup> (2)</span><span class="font49">. Hipotesis nol akan ditolak apabila statistik JB lebih besar daripada nilai </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">χ</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font50">(2)</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Hosking (1990) mengusulkan statistik uji berdasarkan momen-L. Misalkan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font50"><sub>:</sub></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>n</sub></span><span class="font49"> menyatakan statistik terurut tingkat ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49"> dari suatu sampel berukuran </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49">. Definisikan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Statistik pertama yang diusulkan Desmoulins-Lebeault (2004) untuk alternatif kepencongan positif adalah</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font51">∆</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45"> 1<sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50">/ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45"> 2<sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50">/ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">sk</span><span class="font50">). &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(28)</span></p>

<div>
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">(1/2)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45">2:2 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>J, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>3</sub></span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">(1/3)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font50"><sub>3:3</sub> </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">2</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font50"><sub>2:3</sub> </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font50"><sub>1:3</sub>).</span></p>

<p><span class="font49">(23)</span></p>

<div>
<p><span class="font49">Kepencongan-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">L</span><span class="font49"> didefinisikan sebagai </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>3</sub></span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>3</sub>/ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">λ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>2</sub>. </span><span class="font49">Menurut Hosking (1990) statistik</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">[(0,1866</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">0,8</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> <sup>2</sup>)</span><span class="font45">'2</span><span class="font26">∣</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">τ</span><span class="font49"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(24)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">berdistribusi normal.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Bontemps dan Meddahi (2002) mengusulkan model berdasarkan momen rampat (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">generalized method of moments</span><span class="font49">). Misalkan suatu sampel </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> ,</span><span class="font52">K</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font49"> dari peubah acak </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font49"> . <p><span class="font19"><sup>A</sup></span><span class="font45">2 </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font45"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>d</sup></span><span class="font45">3 </span><span class="font50">/ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>σ</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font50"> ) </span><span class="font19"><sup>+ </sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>d</sup></span><span class="font45">42</span><span class="font50">/ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>σ</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">sk</span><span class="font50"> ).</span></p>

<p><span class="font51">A</span><span class="font45">3 </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font45"><sup>(ma</sup></span><span class="font50">x</span><span class="font45"><sup>(|</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font46">+ </span><span class="font50">|,| </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50"> |) </span><span class="font19"><sup>-</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45">5<sup>)2</sup> </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>σ</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font50"> ) </span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font19"><sup>+ </sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>(max(| </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup>4</span><span class="font50"> |,| </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font50"> |) </span><span class="font19"><sup>-</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font45">6</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>σ</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">sk</span><span class="font45">Γ1</span><span class="font50">.</span></p>

<p><span class="font49">(29)</span></p>

<div>
<p><span class="font49">Menurut Desmoulins-Lebeault (2004) distribusi pengambilan sampel pasti dari distribusi semimomen tersebut belumlah diketahui. Oleh karena itu</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Desmoulins-Lebeault (2004) menyediakan tabel nilai kritis untuk masing-masing ukuran sampel.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Lobato dan Velasco (2004) mengusulkan statistik kepencongan dan kurtosis rampat untuk data berkorelasi yakni</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">marjinal </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font49"> adalah </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">N</span><span class="font50">(0,1) </span><span class="font49">. Misalkan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>,</span><span class="font52">K</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f<sub>p </sub></span><span class="font49">adalah fungsi terdiferensialkan sedemikian hingga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> terdeferensialkan. Untuk setiap bilangan real </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49"> dengan komponen </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">xf</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)) </span><span class="font49">untuk </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">1, </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">k</span><span class="font50"> , </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49"> . <p><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">∑ </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font50">+L</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> [ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font50"> ]</span><span class="font49">• (25) dan misalkan pula</span></p>

<div>
<p><span class="font58" style="font-style:italic;">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub></span><span class="font26">∣</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x<sub>i</sub> </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50">med(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50">)|</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">(</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">π</span><span class="font50">/2)</span><span class="font45"><sup>1/2</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50"><sub>3</sub> </span><span class="font49">adalah momen sampel tingkat ketiga, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50">ˆ <sub>4</sub> </span><span class="font49">adalah momen sampel tingkat keempat, </span><span class="font50">med(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">adalah median sampel, nilai </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font50"><sub>2 </sub></span><span class="font49">diperoleh dari simulasi Monte Carlo. Untuk tingkat signifikansi </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">α</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">0,05</span><span class="font49">, Rana </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (2009) merekomendasikan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">6 </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font50"> <sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">64</span><span class="font52" style="font-weight:bold;">.</span></p>

<h5><a name="bookmark134"></a><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><a name="bookmark135"></a>G</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></h5>

<p><span class="font49">dengan &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">d</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">6(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50"> 2) /[(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1)(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">3)]</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">,</span></p>

<div>
<p><span class="font49">1^ </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>, </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">k</span><span class="font50"> , </span><span class="font49">Iw</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">adalah penduga dari nilai tengah asimtotik </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>, </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">k</span><span class="font50"> , </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font50"> )</span><span class="font49">. Statistik</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">BHS </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font49">ι^ </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;"> Σ</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><sub>k</sub></span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font49">ι^ </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font50">)~ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">χ</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50">), </span><span class="font49">(41) dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">Σ</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><sub>k</sub> </span><span class="font49">adalah matriks kovarians dari distribusi bersama ukuran kepencongan dan kurtosis.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Chen dan Kuan (2003) mengusulkan versi uji JB rampat untuk normalitas bersyarat, yakni fungsi nilai tengah bersyarat berisi intersep tetapi tidak bergantung kepada galat masa lalu dan galat bersyarat bersifat heteroskedastik. Statistik yang diusulkan Chen dan Kuan (2003) adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">CH </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50">3]</span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">Σn<sup>1</sup></span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50">3]</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font49">(42) dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> menyatakan banyak sampel, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font58"> <sup>1</sup> ∑^ </span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font49">^, dan </span><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">n<sup>1 </sup></span><span class="font49">adalah penduga konsisten matriks varians-kovarians asimtotik.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Bai dan Ng (2005) mengembangkan uji JB untuk deret waktu atau data tidak bebas. Statistik yang diusulkan Bai dan Ng (2005) adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">π</span><span class="font50"><sub>34</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">π</span><span class="font50"><sub>3</sub> </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">π</span><span class="font50"><sub>4</sub>. </span><span class="font49">(43) Pada persamaan (43) nilai </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">π</span><span class="font50"><sub>3</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>1l2</sup>∕</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">^<sub>3</sub>)/s</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">/</span><span class="font50">Z<sub>3</sub>)</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">π</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>4</sub></span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">π</span><span class="font50"><sub>4</sub>(3) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font50" class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">βΩΩβ</span><span class="font50">/</span><span class="font51" <p><span class="font49">Stfelec dan Stehlik (2009) mengusulkan kelas statistik tangguh JB yang didefinisikan oleh</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">3,54/(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">2)</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">, &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font51"> = -</span><span class="font50">6ln( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font50"> )'ln(</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">π</span><span class="font50"> /2)</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">, &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font45">1/2</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>a</sup></span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font45">i<sup>l </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>x</sup>i</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>- </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>x</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup> l /[</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font58">∑”</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font45">i<sup>(</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>x</sup>i</span><span class="font19"> <sup>- </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>x</sup></span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font45"><sup>]</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50">RT </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">⅛) </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>j</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">Ci </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">m</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;"> α</span><span class="font43"><sup>2</sup>/, </span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font51">k </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font43"> 2</span><span class="font45">,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font43">2 </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">J</span></p>

<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">C</span><span class="font45">2 </span><span class="font51">k </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font45">h.</span></p>

<h2><a name="bookmark144"></a><span class="font19"><sup><a name="bookmark145"></a>- </sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>3</sup></span></h2>
