</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">2.2.2 Beberapa modifikasi statistik uji JB</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font45">,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j. </span><span class="font51">=</span><span class="font45"><sup>(1</sup> </span><span class="font50">∕ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">&quot;</span><span class="font46"> =</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">φ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>j</sub></span><span class="font45"> <sup>(</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X<sub>m</sub></span><span class="font19"> <sup>- </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font45">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font45">)</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font49"><sup>,</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Urzúa (1996) mengusulkan modifikasi uji Jarque-Bera dengan statistik</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50">JBU </span><span class="font51">=</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div><img src="https://jurnal.harianregional.com/media/2908-14.png" alt="" style="width:60pt;height:23pt;">
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50"><sub>3</sub></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(40)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50">{0,1} </span><span class="font49">menyatakan rata-rata aritmetika </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font50"><sub>0</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X </span><span class="font49">atau median </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">M<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50">{0,1,2,3,4} </span><span class="font49">, dan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">φ</span><span class="font50"><sub>0</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">π</span><span class="font50">/2)</span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup>'<sup>2</sup></span><span class="font26">∣</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"> |</span><span class="font52">. </span><span class="font49">Selanjutnya </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">φ</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">φ</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup>, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">φ</span><span class="font50"><sub>3</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"><sup>3</sup>, </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">φ</span><span class="font50"><sub>4</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51"><sup>4</sup> . </span><span class="font49">Nilai </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">C</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">C</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font49">diperoleh dengan simulasi Monte Carlo (lihat Stfelec dan Stehlík,2009).</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Pada persamaan (40) nilai </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">V</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">3(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font50">1)/(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1)</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">6(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50"> 2) /[(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1)(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">3)]</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">, </span><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50"><sub>3</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">24</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50"> 2)(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50"> 3)/[(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1)</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">3)(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">5)]</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Statistik JBU secara asimtotis juga berdistribusi </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">χ</span><span class="font50"> <sup>2</sup>(2)</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Brys </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (2004, 2008) mengamati bahwa uji berdasarkan momen memiliki kelemahan apabila data mengandung pencilan. Selanjutnya Brys </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al. </span><span class="font49">(2004) mengusulkan bentuk statistik uji JB rampat yang mampu menangai pencilan. Misalkan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<h6><a name="bookmark148"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark149"></a>2.3. Uji Kenormalan Berdasarkan Korelasi atau Regresi</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Konsep dasar uji ini adalah plot peluang normal, yaitu teknik grafik untuk menentukan kenormalan data dengan melihat kelinearan dalam suatu plot dari amatan terurut melawan nilai harapan dari statistik terurut normal standar (Lee, 1998). Selanjutnya untuk menentukan kelinearan dapat digunakan teknik regresi atau teknik korelasi. Jika data normal maka kemiringan akan memberikan nilai simpangan baku</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">data dan intersep akan memberikan nilai tengah data</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(Lee,1998).</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">melihat kelemahan statistik SW dan mengusulkan statistik</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Shapiro dan Wilk (1965) mengusulkan statistik</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<h5><a name="bookmark150"></a><span class="font50"><a name="bookmark151"></a>SW </span><span class="font51">-</span></h5>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font58">⅛ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>a</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X^ </span><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font50">( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font50"> )</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(44)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">'</span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font45">,</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1)/2]</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(49)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> menyatakan amatan terurut dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">T / </span><span class="font45" style="font-variant:small-caps;">a</span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mTV</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">a </span><span class="font51">-</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>α</sup></span><span class="font45">,<sup>,</sup></span><span class="font52">K</span><span class="font45"><sup>,</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">(mTv</span><span class="font46">—</span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">1v</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">1m)</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><sub>l</sub></span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">/<sup>2 </sup></span><span class="font50"><sup>,</sup> </span><span class="font48">(45) </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">mT </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>,</span><span class="font52">.</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">menyatakan vektor nilai harapan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">normal standar statistik terurut, </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">V </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v <sub>j</sub></span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">adalah</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">matriks kovarians </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">× </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> , dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">y<sup>T</sup> </span><span class="font51">— </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>,</span><span class="font52">κ</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">U<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50">)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">menyatakan varians sampel.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Modifikasi selanjutnya dilakukan oleh Shapiro dan Francia (1972) yang menyarankan untuk mengabaikan suku kovarians dalam formula untuk mendapatkan berat, yakni memperlakukan amatan terurut seperti halnya saling bebas (lihat juga Dufour </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.,</span><span class="font49"> 1998; Lee, 1998). Statistik yang diusulkan berbentuk</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">menyatakan vektor amatan acak terurut. Jika data normal maka statistik SW akan mendekati 1. Namun,</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<h5><a name="bookmark152"></a><span class="font50"><a name="bookmark153"></a>SF </span><span class="font51">-</span></h5>
</div><br clear="all">
<div><img src="https://jurnal.harianregional.com/media/2908-15.png" alt="" style="width:53pt;height:23pt;">
<p><span class="font50">( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font48">(50)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">jika data tidak normal maka SW akan lebih kecil daripada 1.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Tiku (1974) mengusulkan statistik yang membandingkan simpangan baku sampel dan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">b<sup>T</sup> </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font49"><sub>1</sub>,...,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">c<sup>T</sup>/(c<sup>T</sup>c)<sup>l/2</sup></span><span class="font48">. </span><span class="font49">Statistik SF</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">simpangan baku statistik tersensor. Statistik ini dinyatakan sebagai</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50">TI </span><span class="font7"><sub>-</sub> </span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">(1 </span><span class="font51" style="text-decoration:underline;">- </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">n~<sup>i</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">)σ<sub>c</sub></span></p>
<p><span class="font50">(1 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">nA</span><span class="font50"> )</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(46)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">A </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">—</span><span class="font50"> 1 </span><span class="font51">— </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font51">— </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">q</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub></span><span class="font48">, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font49"> adalah simpangan baku</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">sampel, dan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>c</sub></span><span class="font49"> adalah simpangan baku yang dihitung dari sampel tersensor (lihat Tiku ,1974)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">De Wet dan Venter (1972) mengusulkan statistik uji DW berdasarkan koefisien korelasi sampel antara data dan kuantil distribusi normal standar</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">DW </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">r</span><span class="font50"><sup>2</sup>(</span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">x</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">h</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">(47) dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">r</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">x</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">h</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">adalah koefisien korelasi sampel antar </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">x </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">h </span><span class="font48">. Vektor </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">h </span><span class="font49">pada persamaan (47) adalah vektor berdimensi </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> dengan elemen ke-sama dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> /(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1) </span><span class="font49">kuantil distribusi normal standar.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Filliben (1975) mengusulkan statistik uji FI yang dihitung berdasarkan korelasi antar data dan median statistik terurut ke-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font49">, yakni </span><span class="font50">med(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font50"> )</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font54" style="font-style:italic;">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">FI </span><span class="font7"><sub>-</sub> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">i</span><span class="font3" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sub>-</sub></span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sub>1</sub> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">x<sub>i</sub> </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">-</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">x</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">)(med(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">x<sub>i</sub>) </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">-</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">med(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">x<sub>f</sub></span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">))</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">V∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font3"><sub>-</sub></span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)(med(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">) </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50">med(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">))</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(48)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">2.3.1 Beberapa modifikasi terhadap statistik SW</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Bobot yang diusulkan oleh Shapiro dan Wilk (1965) pada statistik uji (44) adalah berat optimal pendugaan kuadrat terkecil rampat dan sulit dihitung (lihat Dufour, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> 1998). Shapiro dan Wilk (1965) memberikan tabel bobot dan titik-titik signifikan untuk ukuran sampel </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50">50. </span><span class="font49">D’Agostino (1971)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">mengganti </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">V</span><span class="font49"> dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font49"> pada persamaan (50). Selanjutnya Weisberg dan Bingham (1975) memodifikasi statistik SF dengan mengganti nilai </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">c </span><span class="font49">dengan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<h4><a name="bookmark154"></a><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><a name="bookmark155"></a>c</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> - Φ</span></h4>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font45">1</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50"> (3/8) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">(1/4)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50">1,...,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">;</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(51)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font51">Φ</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font49">menyatakan inversi dari fungsi distribusi kumulatif normal (lihat Dufour </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al</span><span class="font49">., 1998; Lee, 1998). Pendekatan ini telah ditunjukkan sesuai untuk sampel kecil.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Sarkadi (1980) mengusulkan untuk melakukan transformasi sebelum menerapkan statistik SW. Lebih lanjut Sarkadi (1980) mengusulkan statistik uji untuk kasus multisampel. Misalkan </span><span class="font48">untuk </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font50">1,</span><span class="font52">.</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">r </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-variant:small-caps;">1,</span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">k</span><span class="font50" style="font-variant:small-caps;">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> peubah </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X<sub>j</sub></span><span class="font49"> menyatakan peubah-peubah acak bebas dengan fungsi distribusi </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">F</span><span class="font50">[(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">μ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub>)/</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ<sub>i</sub>]</span><span class="font49"> dengan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">μ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> tidak diketahui.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Untuk kasus homoskedastik, yakni </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font49"><sub>1</sub> - ... - </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>r</sub> </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">- σ</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan ukuran sampel </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font50">2</span><span class="font48">, </span><span class="font49">Sarkadi (1980)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">mengusulkan statistik dengan transformasi dua tahap, yakni</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">Y</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">- U<sub>1</sub></span><span class="font56" style="font-style:italic;">, </span><span class="font49">dengan</span></p>
<p><span class="font58" style="font-style:italic;">∑ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>1</sup> χ<sub>i</sub> &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">u.</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"> - &nbsp;&nbsp;■ '</span><span class="font49">—-+—</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">in-</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">‘ &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;n</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">+</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup>/<sup>2</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50">)<sup>1/2</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">untuk </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font50">1, </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">k</span><span class="font50"> , </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">r</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">j </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50">1,</span><span class="font52">.</span><span class="font50">, </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">n<sub>i</sub> -</span><span class="font50"> 2</span><span class="font48">.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">melakukan</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">(52)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">(53)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">

<p><span class="font49">Untuk kasus heteroskedastik dengan ukuran sampel </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font50">3 </span><span class="font49">, Sarkadi (1980) mengusulkan statistik</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">Y</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font14">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X<sub>1</sub>- U<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font14">) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">Y^ ij ij i </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(54)</span></p>

<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">Δ-</span><span class="font38" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">∣</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"> i</span><span class="font46" style="text-decoration:underline;">=</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;">1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">j</span></p>

<div>
<h3><a name="bookmark160"></a><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><a name="bookmark161"></a>S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">Y</span><span class="font43" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">Ψ</span></h3>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<h4><a name="bookmark162"></a><span class="font51"><a name="bookmark163"></a>V</span></h4>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">in<sub>i</sub></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">\</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font45">1</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font49"> adalah bilangan bulat positif (lihat Baklizi dan Eidous, 2008).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Arizono, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (1989) mengusulkan uji entropi berdasarkan entropi Renyi. Entropi Renyi didefinisikan oleh</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ψ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>n</sub></span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">adalah fungsi naik tegas sedemikian</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">hingga </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">Y</span><span class="font50"> ~ (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50"> /</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Chen dan Shapiro (1995) dan Chen (2003) memodifikasi statistik SW dan mengusulkan statistik QH berdasarkan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">spacing</span><span class="font49"> yang dinormalkan, yakni</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font50">QH </span><span class="font51">=</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font37" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font37"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;y</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup> -</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>1 </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"><sup>y</sup></span><span class="font46" style="text-decoration:underline;">+</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;">ι </span><span class="font19" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>-</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">y </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">t</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50">1) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font58"> ∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">H<sub>m</sub></span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"> - </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">H</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i’</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(55)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">H<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font51"> =Φ </span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font50">[(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">i —</span><span class="font50"> 3/8)/(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1/4)]</span><span class="font48">, </span><span class="font51">Φ </span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup> </span><span class="font49">adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">inversi distribusi normal standar, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font49"> adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">simpangan baku, dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font49"> adalah statistik terurut. Menurut Seier (2002) uji SW memiliki kelemahan apabila terjadi pembulatan terhadap data. Seier (2002) juga menemukan hal yang sama pada statistik QH dan mengusulkan modifikasi dengan bentuk</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">QH</span><span class="font52">* </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(1 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">QH) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font52"><sup>1/2</sup></span><span class="font50">. </span><span class="font49">(56)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Coin (2008) memodifikasi statistik SW agar mampu menangani pencilan dengan menggunakan pencarian maju (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">forward search</span><span class="font49">). Statistik yang diusulkan Coin (2008) adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">WF</span><span class="font7" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">= </span><span class="font53" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;">(w<sub>s</sub></span><span class="font50"> ,</span><span class="font52">κ</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">W<sub>s</sub></span><span class="font50"> ,</span><span class="font52">κ</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">W<sub>s</sub></span><span class="font17"> )</span><span class="font49">, (57) </span><span class="font43">v </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font43"> [(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font43">+1)/2] ’ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">Sk S^n&gt; <sup>v 7</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S<sub>k</sub></span><span class="font49"> adalah subsampel dari </span><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">x</span><span class="font50"><sub>LMS</sub> </span><span class="font49">yakni penduga regresi kuadrat terkecil dari </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> amatan pertama.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">2.4 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Uji Kenormalan Berdasarkan Entropi Sampel</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Entropi Shannon dari suatu fungsi distribusi </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">F</span><span class="font49"> dengan fungsi densitas peluang </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font49"> didefinisikan sebagai</span></p>
<p><span class="font58">f</span><span class="font46">∞</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)ln</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">) d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font49"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(58)</span></p>
<p><span class="font46">&quot;</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">(lihat Arizono et al., 1998; Park dan Park, 2003; Baklizi dan Eidous, 2008; Choi, 2008). Entropi dari </span><span class="font45">2</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">distribusi normal dengan varians </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font49"> adalah </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">(2</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">π</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font45"> <sup>2</sup>)<sup>1/2</sup></span><span class="font48">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Vasicek (1975) mengusulkan uji entropi sampel dengan statistik uji </span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">exp[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">V</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">x</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;"> , </span><span class="font52" style="text-decoration:underline;">K</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">x</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;"> )] </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font45"> 1</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">, ,</span><span class="font50"> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m,n</span><span class="font50"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;,</span></p>
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>σ</sup></span><span class="font50">( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font45">1<sup>,</sup></span><span class="font52">K</span><span class="font45"><sup>,</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> )</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font49">berdasarkan</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">(59)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">H</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font50"> (.</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(1 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">/</span><span class="font50">l' ln f_[ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)]</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>γ</sup></span><span class="font50"> d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">■</span><span class="font49"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(61)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">/</span><span class="font51"> &gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">/</span><span class="font51"> ≠ </span><span class="font50">1</span><span class="font48">. </span><span class="font49">Entropi ini disebut entropi tingkat </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">/</span><span class="font49"> dari fungsi densitas peluang </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font48">. </span><span class="font49">Apabila </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">γ</span><span class="font51"> → </span><span class="font50">0</span><span class="font48">, </span><span class="font49">entropi Renyi akan tereduksi menjadi entropi Shannon. Selanjutnya Arizono, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (1989) mengusulkan statistik uji berdasarkan entropi Renyi</span></p>
<p><span class="font45">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">H</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">(1 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">/</span><span class="font50">) ln∫<sub>n</sub>[- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">F</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">P </span><span class="font43" style="font-variant:small-caps;">H<sup>1</sup></span><span class="font43" style="font-style:italic;font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>y</sup></span><span class="font50"> d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font50">. </span><span class="font49">(62) </span><span class="font45">0 </span><span class="font50">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">p</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Arizono </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (1989) memperoleh nilai dugaan untuk (62)</span></p>
<p><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">/</span><span class="font45">/(</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">/</span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font45">1)</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">H</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">mn</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">ln </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font58">^ Σ</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font46">+ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X<sub>1</sub></span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t </span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">^</span><span class="font20"> ] </span><span class="font45"><sup>1/(</sup>1—</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">^</span><span class="font45">^)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Choi (2008) mengusulkan statistik uji untuk entropi sampel yang didefinisikan oleh</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">H'.-</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font58"> &nbsp;&nbsp;h </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">‘</span><span class="font49">.Z </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45">(</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font46">+</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">) </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45">(</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">)</span><span class="font49">)] '<sup>,!</sup>. (64)</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font45">1</span></p>
<p><span class="font48">dengan</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R<sub>m</sub></span><span class="font45">, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>n</sub></span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">exp[</span><span class="font51">-</span><span class="font50">(1 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">2 </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50"> / </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n )</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ψ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">(2 m</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ψ</span><span class="font50">( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1)</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">2/</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub></span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">ψ</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font50">1)] &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">( )</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font46">-</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">/(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50">1)]</span><span class="font45"><sup>1/2</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">S</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font48">.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">2.5 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Uji Kenormalan Berdasarkan Karakterisik Polya</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Muliere dan Nikitin (2002) dan Litnova dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Nikitin (2006) mengusulkan dua statistik uji kenormalan berdasarkan karakteristik Polya. Misalkan fungsi distribusi empiris dinyatakan oleh</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup> </span><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font46">=</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">1</span><span class="font50">{</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">t </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">&lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">}, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font49"><sup>1</sup>, &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(66)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan fungsi distribusi statistik-V dinyatakan oleh </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">, </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">=</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font3"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font50"><sup> (</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>m</sup></span><span class="font50"><sup>!)</sup></span><span class="font3"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font58">Σ </span><span class="font15">(</span><span class="font58">∑</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">I</span><span class="font50"><sup>{</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font45">(⅜)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font7"><sup>+</sup> </span><span class="font32">L </span><span class="font7"><sup>+</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">a</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">σ(</span><span class="font43" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>X</sup>m </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">&lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font50"><sup>}</sup></span><span class="font15">) </span><span class="font50"><sup>. </sup></span><span class="font43"><sup>1</sup>'1 </span><span class="font43" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>,</sup></span><span class="font0" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font43" style="font-variant:small-caps;"><sup>, </sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>1</sup>'m</span><span class="font43">=1</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya statistik uji yang diusulkan Litnova dan Nikitin (2006) berbentuk</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">B</span><span class="font45">2,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> =∫</span><span class="font46">&quot; </span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font45">2,</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font51">-</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">)]d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(67)</span></p>
<p><span class="font46">&quot;</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">C</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font45">, </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> =∫&quot;[ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">mn</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50">)] d </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">G</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font50"> )■ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font51"> &gt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">2. </span><span class="font48">(68) </span><span class="font46">&quot;</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font49">untuk </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font27">∈</span><span class="font51"> </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">R</span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font50">.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">

<p><span class="font49">Ahmad dan Mugdadi (2003) mengusulkan metode kernel untuk menguji kenormalan. Misalkan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>, </span><span class="font52">K </span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font49"> adalah sampel acak dari suatu fungsi distribusi </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">F</span><span class="font49"> dengan densitas </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font49">. Misalkan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">u<sub>ii</sub></span><span class="font43">* </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x<sub>i</sub></span><span class="font43">* </span><span class="font49">dengan fungsi densitas peluang </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font48">dan</span></p>

<div>
<h6><a name="bookmark174"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark175"></a>2.7 SIMPULAN</span></h6>
</div><br clear="all">

<h4><a name="bookmark192"></a><span class="font51"><a name="bookmark193"></a>√</span></h4>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font48">(71)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b<sub>n</sub></span><span class="font48"> adalah </span><span class="font49">konstanta positif yang disebut</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">bandwidth</span><span class="font49"> dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font50">(.) </span><span class="font49">adalah densitas terbatas simetrik yang disebut kernel. Diasumsikan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font49"> memiliki nilai tengah 0 dan varians tertentu </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">µ</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font51"> → </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font49">sebagaimana </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> → ∞ </span><span class="font49">. Selanjutnya apabila ingin 2</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">menguji &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">H</span><span class="font49">0 : </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font49"> adalah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">N</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">µ</span><span class="font49">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font49"> ) melawan</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">H<sub>a</sub></span><span class="font50"> : </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">f</span><span class="font50"> bukan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">N</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">µ</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font49">maka ukuran </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font49"> yang</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">didefinisikan oleh</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font58">i</span><span class="font46">∞ r∞</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">u</span><span class="font50">,</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub>(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">u</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">h</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub>(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50">)]</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font50">d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">u</span><span class="font50"> d</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50">, &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font48">(72)</span></p>
<p><span class="font46">-∞ -∞</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">dapat digunakan untuk mengukur kenormalan. Menurut Ahmad dan Mugdadi (2003) </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font51"> ≥ </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font48">dan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">δ</span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">0 </span><span class="font49">jika dan hanya jika hipotesis nol benar. Lebih lanjut Ahmad dan Mugdadi (2003) memperoleh dugaan untuk (72)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50">ˆ</span><span class="font45"><sup>1</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font45"><sup>4</sup></span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50">1)</span><span class="font45"><sup>4</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">u</span><span class="font45"><sub>* *</sub></span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font46">≠</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font46">≠ </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font46">≠</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">l</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">r</span><span class="font46">≠</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">r</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ii jj</span></p>

<div>

<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ii</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">jj</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ll</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">rr</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ii</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">ll</span><span class="font45"><sup>*</sup></span></p>

<div>
<p><span class="font49">dengan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">w</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>u</sup></span></p>

<div>
<h5><a name="bookmark194"></a><span class="font51"><a name="bookmark195"></a>-</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">u</span></h5>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">jj</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<h4><a name="bookmark196"></a><span class="font51"><a name="bookmark197"></a>l</span></h4>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<h4><a name="bookmark198"></a><span class="font51"><a name="bookmark199"></a>√</span></h4>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font48">dan</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(73)</span></p>
<p><span class="font48">(74)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Masing-masing statistik uji kenormalan memiliki keunggulan dan kelemahan masing-masing. Studi komprehensif menunjukkan bahwa uji yang berdasarkan fungsi distribusi empiris secara umum tidak mampu memberikan informasi lain tentang ketidaknormalan. Sebaliknya uji yang berdasarkan momen bersifat omnibus, tetapi tidak terlalu bagus untuk sampel berukuran kecil dan data yang berisi pencilan (lihat Poitras, 2006; Urzúa, 1996; Urzúa, 2007). Uji yang berdasarkan regresi atau korelasi biasanya memerlukan komputasi yang itensif pada saat menentukan bobot. Demikian pula dengan uji-uji yang berdasarkan entropi sampel, kernel, dan karakteristik Polya cenderung memberikan statistik uji yang memerlukan komputasi intensif, terutama simulasi Monte Carlo. Uji kenormalan akan senantiasa berkembang sesuai dengan cara pandang terhadap kenormalan. Sebagai contoh uji kenormalan berdasarkan transformasi proses empiris (Cabaña dan Cabaña, 2003), uji berdasarkan informasi Fisher (Lee, 1998), uji menggunakan statistik Q (Zhang, 1999), dan uji berdasarkan jarak </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">L</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> - Wasserstein </span><span class="font49">(Del Barrio, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al</span><span class="font49">. 1999).</span></p>
