<h6><a name="bookmark202"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark203"></a>MODEL PENYERAPAN OBAT UNTUK INTERVAL DAN DOSIS BERBEDA</span><br><br><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark204"></a>I NYOMAN WIDANA</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Jurusan Matematika, FMIPA, Universitas Udayana Email: </span><a href="mailto:nwidana@yahoo.com"><span class="font49">nwidana@yahoo.com</span></a></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark205"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark206"></a>INTISARI</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">Pada artikel ini akan dibahas akumulasi jumlah obat dalam aliran darah untuk dua metode pemberian obat. Metode pertama obat diberikan setiap 12 jam dengan dosis 12,5 mg, sedangkan metode kedua obat diberikan setiap 24 jam dengan dosis 25 mg. Hasil perhitungan menunjukkan bahwa metode kedua menghasilkan akumulasi jumlah obat dalam aliran darah yang lebih banyak daripada metode pertama.</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Kata kunci: penyerapan obat, dosis obat, akumulasi jumlah obat.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark207"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark208"></a>DRUG ABSORPTION MODEL FOR DIFFERENT INTERVALS AND DOSES</span><br><br><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark209"></a>I NYOMAN WIDANA</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Mathematics Department, FMIPA, Udayana University Email: </span><a href="mailto:nwidana@yahoo.com"><span class="font49">nwidana@yahoo.com</span></a></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark210"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark211"></a>ABSTRACT</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">This article will discuss the accumulated quantity of the drug in the bloodstream of the two administered methods of the drug. The first method the drug is administered every 12 hours with a dose of 12.5 mg, whereas for the second method the drug is administered every 24 hours with a dose of 25 mg. The calculations show that the second method accumulates more drugs in the bloodstream than the first method. SDFLSDKFLSDFSLKFLSKJFSKFLSKFKSDFLKJSLFSLKFSLKFLSKFSLKFLS</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Keywords: drug absorption, drug dose, drug accumulation</span><span class="font48">.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">1. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PENDAHULUAN &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">Misalkan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49">) menyatakan jumlah obat</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Dokter kadang-kadang memberi pilihan kepada pasien untuk meminum obat dua kali sehari dengan dosis tertentu atau satu kali sehari dengan dosis dua kalinya. Untuk itu dalam tulisan ini akan dibahas jumlah obat dalam aliran darah untuk kedua pilihan tersebut.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Tujuan penulisan makalah ini adalah untuk mengetahui akumulasi jumlah obat dalam aliran darah untuk pemberian obat dengan jangka waktu yang lama, khususnya, untuk dua metode pemberian obat. Metode pertama obat diberikan setiap 12 jam dengan dosis 12,5 mg. Sedangkan untuk metode kedua, obat diberikan setiap 24 jam dengan dosis 25 mg. Selain itu akan dibandingkan akumulasi jumlah obat untuk berbagai kecepatan penyerapannya.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark212"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark213"></a>2. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TINJAUAN PUSTAKA</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Studi tentang penurunan konsentrasi obat dalam darah merupakan hal yang vital bagi pasien. Respon dari pasien terhadap dosis obat yang diberikan sangat menentukan dosis yang diperlukan dan interval waktu pemberian obat.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dalam aliran darah pada saat </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49"> . Asumsikan laju perubahannya sebanding dengan konsentrasi obat dalam aliran darah. Hal ini dapat dimodelkan sebagai persamaan diferensial berikut (lihat Burghes dan Borrie,1981; William, 1983)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">dy </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">= - </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">ky</span><span class="font49"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(1)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">dt</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font49"> adalah konstanta positif yang nilainya dapat ditentukan berdasarkan hasil eksperimen terhadap obat yang diteliti.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Misalkan pasien diberikan dosis awal sebesar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"><sub>0 </sub>dan diasumsikan langsung diserap oleh darah pada </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">=</span><span class="font49"> 0, maka hal ini mengakibatkan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"><sub>0</sub> pada saat </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">=</span><span class="font49"> 0. Waktu sebenarnya yang diperlukan untuk penyerapan obat biasanya sangat singkat dibandingkan dengan waktu untuk pemberian dosis berikutnya. Solusi umum dari persamaan (1) adalah </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45"> 0</span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kt</sup></span><span class="font49">. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(2)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Setelah waktu yang ditentukan, misalkan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font49">, dosis kedua sebesar </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"><sub>0</sub> diberikan kepada pasien.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Sesaat sebelum dosis ini diberikan, yaitu pada saat </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">,</span><span class="font49"> jumlah obat dalam darah adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y (T</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45">o</span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font2">-</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Sesaat setelah dosis kedua ini diberikan, pada waktu </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>+</sub></span><span class="font49"> maka</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y (T</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;">+</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45"> o </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45"> o</span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>-kT</sup> </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45"> 0</span><span class="font49">(1</span><span class="font6">+</span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup>T</span><span class="font49">).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Jumlah obat ini menyusut sesuai dengan persamaan (1) dengan kondisi awal </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"><sub>0</sub>(1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font49">) pada saat </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font49">. Sehingga untuk </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font6"> ≥ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font49"> dengan mengingat persamaan (1), diperoleh</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45"> 0</span><span class="font49">(1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font49"> )e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup> (</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup> </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45">)</span><span class="font49">. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(3)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Sehingga, untuk </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font6"> → </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">2T</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y (2T</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45"> 0</span><span class="font49">(1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font49"> )e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya setelah memberikan pasien dosis </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"><sub>0 </sub>pada waktu </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49">2</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font49"> diperoleh</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"> (2</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font2">+ </span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45"> 0</span><span class="font49">(1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font6"> + </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-2 </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font49"> )</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan sekali lagi dengan menggunakan persamaan (1) dengan </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"><sub>0</sub>(1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">e“</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font6"> + </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-2</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font49"> ) pada saat </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">2T</span><span class="font49">, diperoleh</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"><sub>0</sub>(1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup>T</span><span class="font6"> + </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-2</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup>T</span><span class="font49"> )e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>-2</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>T</sup></span><span class="font45">)</span><span class="font49">, &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;untuk </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font6"> ≥ </span><span class="font49">2</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Dengan jalan yang sama,</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"> (3</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font2">- </span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45"> 0</span><span class="font49">(1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font6"> + </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-2 </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font49"> )e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font49">,</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan setelah diberi dosis </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"><sub>0</sub> pada </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font6"> = </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">3T</span><span class="font49"> ,</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y (3T</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>+</sub></span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"> <sub>0</sub>(1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font6"> + </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-2 </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font6"> + </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-3 </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font49"> ).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya, diperoleh</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"> (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">nT</span><span class="font2" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>+</sub></span><span class="font49"> ) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font49"> <sub>0</sub>(1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup>T</span><span class="font6"> + </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-2 </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup>T</span><span class="font6"> + </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-3 </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup>T</span><span class="font6"> + </span><span class="font35" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l</span><span class="font6"> + </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>nkT</sup></span><span class="font49"> ), </span><span class="font50">untuk </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">1,2, </span><span class="font36" style="font-variant:small-caps;">k</span><span class="font48"> .</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Kemudian menggunakan deret geometri diperoleh</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">+</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">=</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45"> 0</span><span class="font50">(1 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>( </sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>1)</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kT</sup></span><span class="font50">) 1-e</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>-kT</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan untuk </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font49"> yang makin besar, diperoleh</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">nT</span><span class="font46" style="font-style:italic;">+</span><span class="font50">) </span><span class="font51">→ </span><span class="font45"><sub>1</sub></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>y</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font49">Dari model ini diperoleh bahwa jumlah obat dalam darah akan mencapai tingkat kejenuhan, </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y<sub>j</sub></span><span class="font49"> dengan</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font51"> =</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font50"><sub>0 </sub>1-e</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>-kT</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(4)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark214"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark215"></a>3. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PENYERAPAN OBAT</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Misalkan pasien diberikan obat dengan dosis 12,5 mg setiap 12 jam (1/2 hari) maka, dari persamaan (2), diperoleh jumlah obat dalam darah adalah</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">12,5e</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kt</sup></span><span class="font50">, 0 </span><span class="font51">≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font51"> ≤ ⅜.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Berdasarkan persamaan (3), diperoleh </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45">1</span><span class="font49">(</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font49">) </span><span class="font6">= </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font45">01</span><span class="font49">(1 </span><span class="font6">+ </span><span class="font49">e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup>T</span><span class="font49"> )e</span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>t</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">T</span><span class="font45">)</span><span class="font49">, </span><span class="font45">⅜ </span><span class="font6">≤ </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font6"> &lt;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">1.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Sedangkan untuk pengobatan dengan dosis 25 mg setiap 24 jam (1 hari) diperoleh</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y</span><span class="font50"> <sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">25e</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>kt</sup></span><span class="font50">, 0 </span><span class="font51">≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">t</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50">1</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Untuk </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">1, </span><span class="font49">jumlah obat dalam darah untuk dosis</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">12,5 mg dan 25 mg diilustrasikan oleh grafik berikut</span></p><img src="https://jurnal.harianregional.com/media/2908-16.png" alt="" style="width:187pt;height:187pt;">
<p><span class="font48">Gambar 1. Jumlah obat dalam aliran darah untuk </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">1.</span></p>
<div>
<p><span class="font49">Sedangkan untuk </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">5 </span><span class="font49">, jumlah obat dalam darah dapat dilihat pada grafik berikut</span></p><img src="https://jurnal.harianregional.com/media/2908-17.png" alt="" style="width:191pt;height:191pt;">
<p><span class="font48">Gambar 2. Jumlah obat dalam aliran darah untuk </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">5.</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya akan dibahas jumlah obat dalam aliran darah dalam jangka waktu yang lama untuk kedua metode diatas. Metode 1, pasien diberikan obat dengan dosis 12,5 mg setiap 12 jam (1/2 hari), maka jumlah obat dalam darah dalam jangka waktu yang lama, dengan menggunkan persamaan (4), akan mencapai</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">12,5</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>y</sup>j</span><span class="font49"><sup>1</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1 p-</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font45">/2 </span><span class="font50">. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(<sup>5</sup>)</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">1 e</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Untuk metode 2, pengobatan dilakukan dengan dosis 25 mg setiap 24 jam (1 hari), sehingga dengan jalan yang sama diperoleh</span></p>
<div>
<h3><a name="bookmark216"></a><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><a name="bookmark217"></a>y</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j2</span><span class="font51"> =</span></h3>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font50">25</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">1 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">e</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup> .</sup></span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<div>
<p><span class="font49">(6)</span></p>
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font49">Jumlah obat dalam darah untuk kedua metode tersebut, untuk </span><span class="font50">1 </span><span class="font51">≤ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font51"> ≤ </span><span class="font50">5</span><span class="font49">, diilustrasikan oleh grafik berikut</span></p>
<div><img src="https://jurnal.harianregional.com/media/2908-18.png" alt="" style="width:134pt;height:84pt;">
</div><br clear="all">
<p><span class="font43">---------- Metode 1</span></p>
<p><span class="font43"><sup>a</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Metode 2</span></p>
<p><span class="font48">Gambar 3. Jumlah obat dalam aliran darah untuk 1 </span><span class="font36">≤ </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">k</span><span class="font36"> ≤ </span><span class="font48">5.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Selanjutnya, dapat ditunjukkan bahwa</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">12,5 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;25</span></p>
<h4><a name="bookmark218"></a><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;"><a name="bookmark219"></a>y</span><span class="font51">,i =-----■ &lt;-----r = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">y i</span><span class="font51"> 2, </span><span class="font50">untuk </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">k </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">&gt;</span><span class="font50">&nbsp;0.</span></h4>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font43"><sup>1</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">1 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">e</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup></span><span class="font43">/2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">1 </span><span class="font51">- </span><span class="font50">e</span><span class="font37"><sup>-</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>k</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">j</span><span class="font43"> <sup>2</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Hal ini berarti bahwa dalam jangka waktu yang lama, jumlah obat dalam aliran darah, untuk metode 1, lebih sedikit dari jumlah obat dalam aliran darah untuk metode 2.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark220"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark221"></a>4. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SIMPULAN</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Pemberian obat setiap 24 jam dengan dosis 25 mg menghasilkan akumulasi jumlah obat dalam aliran darah yang lebih banyak daripada pemberian obat setiap 12 jam dengan dosis 12,5 mg, untuk pemberian obat dengan jangka waktu yang lama.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark222"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark223"></a>DAFTAR PUSTAKA</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">Burghes, D. N. and Borrie, M. S. 1981. </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Modelling with Differential</span><span class="font48"> Equation. Ellis Horwood Limited. London.</span></p>
<p><span class="font48">William, F. L. 1983. </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Differential Equation</span><span class="font48"> Models. Springer-Verlag. New York.</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-weight:bold;">IMPLEMENTASI BEBERAPA UJI KENORMALAN OMNIBUS DENGAN PERANGKAT LUNAK R</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">I WAYAN SUMARJAYA</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Jurusan Matematika, FMIPA, Universitas Udayana Email: </span><a href="mailto:sumarjaya@unud.ac.id"><span class="font49">sumarjaya@unud.ac.id</span></a></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark224"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark225"></a>INTISARI</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">Uji kenormalan omnibus adalah ujian kenormalan yang mampu memberikan informasi tambahan tentang ketidaknormalan data atau penyimpangannya melalui koefisien kepencongan dan kurtosis. Penelitian ini bertujuan untuk mengimplementasikan penghitungan statistik uji kenormalan omnibus D’Agostino-Pearson </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font48"><sup>2</sup> dan statistik uji modifikasi Jarque-Bera menggunakan perangkat lunak R.sfdsdfsfsfsdfs sdfdsfsfssfsfsdfsd &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;dfsdllflsdflskdflsklfkslfksdllskflskflsllsdfs</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Kata kunci: uji kenormalan omnibus, uji D’Agostino-Pearson, uji Jarque-Bera termodifikasi.</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark226"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark227"></a>IMPLEMENTATION OF SOME OMNIBUS NORMALITY TEST USING R SOFTWARE</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">I WAYAN SUMARJAYA</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Mathematics Department, FMIPA, Udayana University Email: </span><a href="mailto:sumarjaya@unud.ac.id"><span class="font49">sumarjaya@unud.ac.id</span></a></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark228"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark229"></a>ABSTRACT</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">An omnibus normality test is a normality test that can give additional information about nonnormality or other deviation from normality through the skewness and the kurtosis coefficients. The aim of this research is to implement the omnibus D’Agostino-Pearson </span><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font48"><sup>2</sup> test and modified Jarque-Bera test statistic using R software. ssdkflsfjlskdflskjflskflskflskflskfksflksjfkslfksfksfslkfslkfslfsfsfssss.sdflsfl</span></p>
<p><span class="font48" style="font-style:italic;">Keywords: omnibus normality test, D’Agostino-Pearson test, modified Jarque-Bera</span><span class="font48">.</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark230"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark231"></a>1. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PENDAHULUAN</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Uji kenormalan telah menarik banyak perhatian para peneliti. Telah ratusan tulisan ilmiah tentang uji kenormalan dipublikasikan. Secara umum uji kenormalan dapat dikelompokkan ke dalam beberapa jenis: uji berdasarkan fungsi distribusi empiris, uji berdasarkan momen, uji berdasarkan korelasi atau regresi, uji berdasarkan entropi sampel, uji berdasarkan karakteristik Polya, uji berdasarkan metode kernel, dan uji berdasarkan metode nonparametrik.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Studi komprehensif yang dilakukan Stephens (1972), Koziol (1986), Dufour </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49">(1998), Seier (2002), Coin dan Corradetti (2006), Farrell dan Rogers-Stewart (2006), Breton </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (2008) Yazici and Yolacan (2007), Tanweer-ul-Islam (2008), Tanweer-ul-Islam dan Zaman (2008) menunjukkan bahwa masing-masing statistik uji memiliki keunggulan dan kelemahan. Sebagai contoh uji yang berdasarkan fungsi distribusi empiris atau uji jarak umumnya tidak mampu memberikan informasi tambahan tentang ketidaknormalan distribusi alternatif. Uji yang berdasarkan regresi atau korelasi</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">biasanya memerlukan komputasi yang itensif pada saat menentukan bobot. Demikian pula dengan uji-uji yang berdasarkan entropi sampel, kernel, dan karakteristik Polya cenderung memberikan statistik uji yang memerlukan komputasi intensif, terutama simulasi Monte Carlo.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Statistik uji yang mampu memberikan informasi tambahan tentang ketidaknormalan atau penyimpangan dari kenormalan disebut uji omnibus. Uji ini biasanya melaporkan koefisien kepencongan dan kurtosis sebagai ukuran untuk mengetahui normal atau tidaknya data.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Penelitian ini membahas implementasi statistik uji kenormalan omnibus D’Agostino-Pearson </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font45"><sup>2 </sup></span><span class="font49">(lihat D’Agostino, </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al</span><span class="font49">. 1990) dan modifikasi uji Jarque-Bera yang diusulkan oleh Urzúa (1996, 2007)</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<h6><a name="bookmark232"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark233"></a>2. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;METODE-METODE UJI KENORMALAN OMNIBUS</span></h6></li></ul>
<p><span class="font49">Konsep uji berdasarkan momen adalah bahwa momen ketiga dan momen keempat yang diberikan oleh</span></p>
<table border="1">
<tr><td style="vertical-align:bottom;">
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>β</sub></span><span class="font51"> _ &nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">E</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">X</span><span class="font51" style="text-decoration:underline;"> - </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">μ</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">)</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>3</sup></span><span class="font45"> &nbsp;</span><span class="font51">_ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">E</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">X</span><span class="font51" style="text-decoration:underline;"> - </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">μ</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">)</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font45"> &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(1)</span></p>
<p><span class="font45">'<sup>j1</sup> &nbsp;</span><span class="font50">[</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">μ</span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font50">)T</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">σ<sup>3 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;U</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;"><sub>β</sub></span><span class="font51"> _ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">E</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">X</span><span class="font51" style="text-decoration:underline;"> - </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">μ</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">)</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;">4</span><span class="font45"> </span><span class="font51">_ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">E</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">X</span><span class="font51" style="text-decoration:underline;"> - </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">μ</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">)</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;">4</span></p>
<p><span class="font45"><sup>P2</sup> &nbsp;</span><span class="font50">[ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">μ</span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50">]</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">σ<sup>4</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;°</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dari distribusi </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">N</span><span class="font50">(0,1) </span><span class="font49">adalah 0 dan 3. Konsep momen ini dimunculkan pertama kali oleh Karl Pearson. Selanjutnya, momen ketiga disebut kepencongan (</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">skewness</span><span class="font49">) dan momen keempat disebut kurtosis. Dengan demikian penyimpangan dari kenormalan dapat diketahui dari nilai momen-momen yang diduga menggunakan sampel, yakni koefisien kepencongan &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">dan koefisien kurtosis</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font49">yang dihitung sebagai</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b<sup>h</sup></span><span class="font11"> = (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m')</span><span class="font45"> 3/2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49"><sup>(3)</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> ) </span><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>b</sup>2</span><span class="font51"> = &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(4)</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub>)</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dengan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">m<sub>j</sub></span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">(1/ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font58" style="text-decoration:underline;">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;">”</span><span class="font50"> (</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">x<sub>i</sub> - </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>j</sup></span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Kepencongan dan kurtosis dapat diukur dengan lebih dari satu cara. Fisher (lihat D’Agostino </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49">, 1990) mendefinisikan kepencongan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">dan kurtosis </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font49">sebagai</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font58" style="text-decoration:underline;"> ∑</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;">'1</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">x</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">i</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"><sup>- </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"><sup>x</sup></span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;"> &gt;</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>3</sup></span><span class="font45"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(5)</span></p>
<p><span class="font45"><sup>S1</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50">1)( </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50"> 2) </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s<sup>3</sup>’</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">(</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font51" style="text-decoration:underline;"> +</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>1</sup></span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">)</span><span class="font58" style="text-decoration:underline;">∑</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">&quot;</span><span class="font46" style="text-decoration:underline;">=</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sub>1</sub>(</span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"><sup>x</sup>i</span><span class="font19" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>- </sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;"><sup>x</sup></span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>)4</sup></span><span class="font45"> </span><span class="font7"><sub>-</sub> </span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">3(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">-</span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:underline;">1)</span><span class="font45" style="text-decoration:underline;"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font45"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49"><sub>(6)</sub></span></p>
<p><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>g</sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font50">1)(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50">2)(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50">3)</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s<sup>4</sup> </span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50">2)(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50">3), </span><span class="font49"><sup>(</sup> ) dengan</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">_ &nbsp;&nbsp;y</span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>n</sup></span><span class="font50"> <sub>ι</sub>(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font51">-</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font50">)<sup>2</sup></span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">s</span><span class="font45"> 2 </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font49">∑⅛A----</span><span class="font50" style="font-variant:small-caps;">l.</span><span class="font49"> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(7)</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> -</span><span class="font50">1)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Geary (lihat Bonnet dan Seier, 2002) mendefinisikan kurtosis sebagai </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">τ</span><span class="font50"> / </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font49"> dengan </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">τ</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">E</span><span class="font50">(| </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">μ</span><span class="font50"> |) </span><span class="font49">. Lebih lanjut, menurut Bonnet dan Seier (2002) pada kondisi kenormalan dapat ditunjukkan bahwa </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">τ</span><span class="font50"> / </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">σ</span><span class="font51"> = </span><span class="font50">(2/</span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">^</span><span class="font50">)</span><span class="font45"><sup>1/2</sup></span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">0,7979. </span><span class="font49">Pembahasan lebih lanjut tentang kepencongan dan</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;">
<p><span class="font49">yang berdistribusi </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">χ</span><span class="font50"> <sup>2</sup>(2) </span><span class="font49">apabila populasi berdistribusi normal. Pada persamaan (8) nilai </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">Z</span><span class="font31"><sup>2</sup> (∙∖</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font31">) </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">Z</span><span class="font11"><sup>2</sup> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"> <sub>2</sub></span><span class="font11">) </span><span class="font49">adalah pendekatan-pendekatan normal terhadap </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">dan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font49">. Hipotesis dan langkah-langkah pengujian terhadap kepencongan, kurtosis, dan statistik </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font45"> <sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font49">dapat dilihat pada D’Agostino </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (1990).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">2.2 Uji Omnibus Jarque-Bera</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Pendekatan pengujian menggunakan kepencongan </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font49">dan kurtosis </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font49">juga diusulkan oleh Jarque dan Bera (1980, 1987) dan Bera dan Jarque (1981) dengan statistik uji</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">J</span><span class="font45"><sup>B</sup> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> [<sup>()</sup></span><span class="font19"><sup>+ </sup></span><span class="font45"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font45" style="font-style:italic;"><sup>b</sup></span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font50">243) </span><span class="font51">j &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(9)</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Statistik JB secara asimtotis berdistribusi </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">χ</span><span class="font45">2</span><span class="font50">(2)</span><span class="font49">. Hipotesis nol akan ditolak apabila statistik JB lebih besar daripada nilai </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">χ</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font50">(2)</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Urzúa (1996) melihat kelemahan uji Jarque-Bera untuk sampel berukuran kecil sampai menengah dan mengusulkan modifikasi uji Jarque-Bera dengan statistik</span></p>
<p><span class="font50">JBU =L</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font50">I </span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:line-through;"><sup>(</sup></span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:line-through;"><sup>b</sup></span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:line-through;"><sup>2 </sup></span><span class="font7" style="text-decoration:line-through;"><sup>-</sup> </span><span class="font50" style="text-decoration:line-through;">^<sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50"> . &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(10)</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font45"> 2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font45">3</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Pada persamaan (10) nilai</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50"><sub>1</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">3(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50">1)/(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1)</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">,</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50"><sub>2</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">6(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">-</span><span class="font50"> 2) /[(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1)(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">3)]</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">, </span><span class="font49">dan</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">v</span><span class="font50"><sub>3</sub> </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">24</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50">2)(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> - </span><span class="font50">3)/[(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> +</span><span class="font50">1)</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span><span class="font50">(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">3)(</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">n</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">5)]</span><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Statistik JBU secara asimtotis juga berdistribusi </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">X</span><span class="font50"><sup>2</sup>(2)</span><span class="font49">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Urzúa (2007) mengusulkan dua uji omnibus untuk kenormalan menggunakan ukuran kepencongan Pearson dan kurtosis Geary, yakni statistik</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">U</span><span class="font45">1 </span><span class="font51" style="font-style:italic;">= </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">UbL</span><span class="font51"> + </span><span class="font50">C</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">^</span><span class="font51">-</span><span class="font45"><sup>32</sup> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(11)</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">de</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">dan</span></p></td></tr>
<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font49">kurtosis dapat dilihat pada DeCarlo (1997).</span></p>
<p><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;">2.1 Uji Omnibus D’Agostino-Pearson </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font45"><sup>2</sup></span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;">
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">U</span><span class="font45">2 </span><span class="font51">= </span><span class="font50">max &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<sub>r</sub> ) . &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="font49">(12)</span></p>

<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font49">D’Agostino dan Pearson mengusulkan statistik uji menggunakan momen Pearson (lihat D’Agostino </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al</span><span class="font49">., 1990)</span></p>
<p><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font51"><sup>2</sup> = </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">Z</span><span class="font31"><sup>2</sup> (√</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font31">)</span><span class="font51">+ </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">Z</span><span class="font31"><sup>2</sup> (</span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">b</span><span class="font51">2</span><span class="font31">)</span><span class="font49">, (8)</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;">

<h6><a name="bookmark234"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark235"></a>IMPLEMENTASI UJI KENORMALN OMNIBUS</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Berikut ini implementasi uji omnibus D’Agostino-Pearson </span><span class="font50" style="font-style:italic;">K</span><span class="font45"> <sup>2</sup> </span><span class="font49">berdasarkan D’Agostino </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">et al.</span><span class="font49"> (1990).</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font34"># &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;fungsi DAP menghitung kepencongan,</span></p></li>
<li>
<p><span class="font34"># &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;kurtosis</span></p></li>
<li>
<p><span class="font34"># &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;dan statistik K^2</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font34">DAP.omnibus &lt;- function(x,alpha){ n &lt;- length(x) m2 &lt;- sum((x - mean(x))^2)/n</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">m3 &lt;- sum((x - mean(x))^3)/n</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">m4 &lt;- sum((x - mean(x))^4)/n</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font34"># # prosedur pengujian kepencongan sqrt.b1 &lt;- m3/(m2^1.5) cat(&quot;Kepencongan sampel:&quot;,sqrt.b1,&quot;\n&quot;) a1 &lt;- (n + 1)*(n + 3) a2 &lt;- 6*(n - 2)</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font34">Y &lt;- sqrt.b1*sqrt(a1/a2)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">a3 &lt;- 3*(n^2 + 27*n - 70)*(n + 1)*(n + 3)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">a4 &lt;- (n - 2)*(n + 5)*(n + 7)*(n + 9) betatwo.sqrt.b1 &lt;- a3/a4</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">sqr.W &lt;- -1 + sqrt(2*betatwo.sqrt.b1 -</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">1)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">W &lt;- sqrt(sqr.W)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">delta &lt;- 1/sqrt(log(W))</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">alpha &lt;- sqrt(2/(sqr.W - 1))</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">Z.sqrt.b1 &lt;- delta*log(Y/alpha + sqrt((Y/alpha)^2 + 1))</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">cat(&quot;Statistik uji</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">kepencongan:&quot;,Z.sqrt.b1,&quot;\n&quot;)</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font34"># # prosedur pengujian kurtosis</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font34">b2 &lt;- m4/(m2^2)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">cat(&quot;Kurtosis sampel:&quot;,b2,&quot;\n&quot;) a5 &lt;- 3*(n - 1) a6 &lt;- (n + 1)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">E.b2 &lt;- a5/a6</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">a7 &lt;- 24*n*(n-2)*(n - 3)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">a8 &lt;- ((n + 1)^2)*(n + 3)*(n + 5) var.b2 &lt;- a7/a8</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">x &lt;- (b2 - E.b2)/(sqrt(var.b2)) a9 &lt;- 6*(n^2 - 5*n + 2) a10 &lt;- (n + 7)*(n + 9) a11 &lt;- 6*(n + 3)*(n + 5) a12 &lt;- n*(n - 2)*(n - 3) sqrt.betaone.b2 &lt;-</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">(a9/a10)*sqrt(a11/a12)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">a13 &lt;- 8/sqrt.betaone.b2</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">a14 &lt;- 2/sqrt.betaone.b2</span></p>
<table border="1">
<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">a15</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">&lt;- 1</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">+ (4/sqrt.betaone.b2)</span></p></td></tr>
<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">A &lt;-</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">6 +</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">a13*(a14 + sqrt(a15))</span></p></td></tr>
<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">a16</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">&lt;- 1</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">- (2/(9*A))</span></p></td></tr>
<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">a17</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">&lt;- 1</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">- 2/A</span></p></td></tr>
<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">a18</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">&lt;- 1</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">+ x*sqrt(2/(A - 4))</span></p></td></tr>
<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">a19</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">&lt;- s</span></p></td><td style="vertical-align:top;">
<p><span class="font34">qrt(2/(9*A))</span></p></td></tr>
</table>
<p><span class="font34">Z.b2 &lt;- (a16 - (a17/a18)^(1/3))/(a19) cat(&quot;Statistik uji</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">kurtosis:&quot;,Z.b2,&quot;\n&quot;)</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font34"># # prosedur pengujian omnibus K^2 sqr.K &lt;- (Z.sqrt.b1)^2 + (Z.b2)^2 cat(&quot;Statistik uji Agostino-Pearson K</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font34">kuadrat:&quot;,sqr.K,&quot;\n&quot;)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">if (sqr.K &gt;= qchisq(1-alpha,2)) { cat(&quot;Hipotesis nol ditolak.&quot;,&quot;\n&quot;)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">} else {</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">cat(&quot;Hipotesis nol tidak ditolak.&quot;</span><span class="font34" style="font-weight:bold;">, </span><span class="font34">&quot;\n&quot;)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">}</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">}</span></p>
<p><span class="font49">Implementasi statistik uji modifikasi Jarque-Bera oleh Urzúa (1996).</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font34"># &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;fungsi JBU omnibus mengimplementasikan</span></p></li>
<li>
<p><span class="font34"># &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;modifikasi Jarque-Bera oleh Urzua</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font34">JBU.omnibus &lt;- function(x,alpha){</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">n &lt;- length(x)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">m2 &lt;- sum((x - mean(x))^2)/n</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">m3 &lt;- sum((x - mean(x))^3)/n</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">m4 &lt;- sum((x - mean(x))^4)/n sqrt.b1 &lt;- m3/(m2^1.5) v1 &lt;- 3*(n - 1)/(n + 1)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">v2 &lt;- 6*(n - 2)/((n + 1)*(n + 3))</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">v3 &lt;- 24*n*(n - 2)*(n - 3)/</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">((n + 1)^2*(n + 3)*(n + 5))</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">b2 &lt;- m4/(m2^2)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">JBU &lt;- (sqrt.b1)^2/(v2) + (b2-v1)/(v3) cat(&quot;Nilai statistik JBU:&quot;,JBU,&quot;\n&quot;) if (JBU &gt;= qchisq(1-alpha,2)) {</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">cat(&quot;Hipotesis nol ditolak.&quot;,&quot;\n&quot;)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">} else {</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">cat(&quot;Hipotesis nol tidak ditolak.&quot;</span><span class="font34" style="font-weight:bold;">, </span><span class="font34">&quot;\n&quot;)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">}</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">}</span></p>
<ul style="list-style:none;"><li>
<p><span class="font34"># &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Statistik Urzua (2007)</span></p></li></ul>
<p><span class="font34">U.omnibus &lt;- function(x,alpha){</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">n &lt;- length(x)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">m2 &lt;- sum((x - mean(x))^2)/n</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">m3 &lt;- sum((x - mean(x))^3)/n</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">m4 &lt;- sum((x - mean(x))^4)/n sqrt.b1 &lt;- m3/(m2^1.5)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">d &lt;- 6*(n-2)/((n + 1)*(n + 3))</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">e &lt;- 3.54/(n + 2)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">a &lt;- sum(abs(x - mean(x)))/n*sum((x-mean(x)))</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">w &lt;- -6*log(a)/log(pi/2)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">U1 &lt;- (sqrt.b1/d) + (w - 3)^2/e</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">U2 &lt;- max(sqrt.b1/d,(w - 3)/sqrt(e)) cat(&quot;Nilai statistik U1:&quot;,U1,&quot;\n&quot;) cat(&quot;Nilai statistik U2:&quot;,U2,&quot;\n&quot;) if (U1 &gt;= qchisq(1-alpha,2)) {</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">cat(&quot;Hipotesis nol ditolak.&quot;,&quot;\n&quot;)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">} else {</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">cat(&quot;Hipotesis nol tidak ditolak.&quot;</span><span class="font34" style="font-weight:bold;">, </span><span class="font34">&quot;\n&quot;)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">}</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">if (U2 &gt;= 2.236) { %% alfa 5% cat(&quot;Hipotesis nol ditolak.&quot;,&quot;\n&quot;) } else {</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">cat(&quot;Hipotesis nol tidak ditolak.&quot;</span><span class="font34" style="font-weight:bold;">, </span><span class="font34">&quot;\n&quot;)</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">}</span></p>
<p><span class="font34">}</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark236"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark237"></a>SIMPULAN</span></h6>
<p><span class="font49">Implementasi uji omnibus di atas perlu disempuranakan lagi untuk menghitung </span><span class="font49" style="font-style:italic;">p</span><span class="font49">-value dan antisipasi terhadap data yang mengandung nol (0).</span></p>
<h6><a name="bookmark238"></a><span class="font49" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark239"></a>DAFTAR PUSTAKA</span></h6>
<p><span class="font48">Bera, A. K. and Jarque, C. M. 1981.
